# 如何以“陛下终于下旨，说要诛我九族”为开头，写一个故事？
- 点赞数：69346
- 更新时间：2024年03月19日16时35分29秒
- 回答url：https://www.zhihu.com/question/436040578/answer/1642101497
<body>
 <blockquote>
  《地府之前》
 </blockquote>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>1<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>陛下终于下旨<span><span>，</span></span>说要诛我九族<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我实在太高兴了<span><span>，</span></span>在屋内忍不住想要大叫<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这次任务结束<span><span>，</span></span>我就可以回到地府<span><span>，</span></span>继续做我的押魂使<span><span>。</span></span>天知道为了完成阎王给的这劳什子任务<span><span>，</span></span>我在人间已经待了多久<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>十八年<span><span>！</span></span>十八年啊朋友们<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>在做人以前<span><span>，</span></span>我从未想过人间时间过得如此之慢<span><span>。</span></span>我以为人嘛<span><span>，</span></span>区区几十年寿命<span><span>，</span></span>一眨眼也就过了<span><span>。</span></span>所以当阎王发任务的时候<span><span>，</span></span>我自告奋勇<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>昔日<span><span>，</span></span>我威风凛凛<span><span>，</span></span>如今<span><span>，</span></span>我悔不当初<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可今日<span><span>，</span></span>我太兴奋了<span><span>，</span></span>我终于要完成任务<span><span>，</span></span>功成身退了<span><span>。</span></span>房间内<span><span>，</span></span>我扒在门上<span><span>、</span></span>窗户上<span><span>，</span></span>四下确认无人<span><span>，</span></span>便摸着颈间玉佩<span><span>，</span></span>低声儿唤道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>大人…大人…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我叫了许久<span><span>，</span></span>玉佩那边才传来懒散的声音<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>说…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我压着嗓子<span><span>，</span></span>可压不住内心的兴奋<span><span>，</span></span>声音透着一股难以掩饰的欣喜若狂<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姜叶颂终于要被诛九族啦<span><span>！</span></span>我马上就能回地府了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 阎王大人极其敷衍<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何时<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我回道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>传闻<span><span>，</span></span>午后会来下旨<span><span>，</span></span>秋后执行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那也就是说还没接到圣旨…<span><span>」</span></span> 阎王觉得我又在传递虚假信息<span><span>，</span></span>于是十分不耐烦<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不不不…<span><span>」</span></span> 我连忙道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这次八九不离十<span><span>。</span></span>姜叶颂她弟弟造反<span><span>，</span></span>已经被逮了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦…<span><span>」</span></span> 阎王声音平淡<span><span>，</span></span>好似对这些凡尘事已经见怪不怪<span><span>。</span></span>他又<span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>」</span></span>了一声儿<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>既然如此<span><span>，</span></span>那我们就秋后黄泉相见了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这话说完<span><span>，</span></span>阎王便消失了<span><span>。</span></span>任我如何找他<span><span>，</span></span>他都未曾再应过一句话<span><span>。</span></span>几日后<span><span>，</span></span>在大牢里<span><span>，</span></span>趁着万籁俱寂<span><span>，</span></span>我悄悄问了地府的其他鬼差<span><span>，</span></span>才知道地府忙了起来<span><span>，</span></span>阎王张罗着<span><span>，</span></span>大张旗鼓地要迎接什么人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>害…</p>
 <p>怪是不好意思的<span><span>。</span></span>都是老鬼了<span><span>，</span></span>也不是没见过<span><span>，</span></span>又不是很久没见<span><span>，</span></span>不过一十八年<span><span>，</span></span>何至于此<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我暗暗扒拉手指头<span><span>，</span></span>算着回地府的日子<span><span>。</span></span>若是幸运<span><span>，</span></span>兴许赶得上这个月的鬼市<span><span>，</span></span>再巧一些<span><span>，</span></span>阎王大人冥诞也赶得上<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我琢磨得好好的<span><span>，</span></span>可是行刑前的夜里出了岔子<span><span>。</span></span>不知哪个不要命的<span><span>，</span></span>撂倒了所有狱卒<span><span>，</span></span>要带我逃走<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我不走<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>彼时<span><span>，</span></span>我十分决绝<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>眼看着临门一脚<span><span>，</span></span>谁跟他走谁是傻子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那人挺惊讶<span><span>，</span></span>眼珠子盯着我看了好一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>最终一掌下来劈昏了我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>害…</p>
 <p>人类的肉体<span><span>，</span></span>就是如此脆弱<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>2<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>我醒来的时候<span><span>，</span></span>已经是第二天<span><span>。</span></span>时候不早了<span><span>，</span></span>估计着该斩首的也斩首得差不多了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我呆呆坐在榻上<span><span>，</span></span>生无可恋<span><span>，</span></span>死也赶不上趟儿<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不行…我要死<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>信念坚决<span><span>，</span></span>我迅速下榻<span><span>，</span></span>屋里屋外找寻着趁手的兵器<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>让人生气的是<span><span>，</span></span>这屋里屋外<span><span>，</span></span>连房梁上我都爬着瞧了<span><span>，</span></span>愣是连个绳子都没有<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>撞墙<span><span>？</span></span>我心生一计<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可四下一看<span><span>，</span></span>竟是个茅草屋<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>茅草屋…能撞死人么<span><span>？</span></span>这个问题我考虑了许久<span><span>。</span></span>我真的不想撞不死<span><span>，</span></span>反撞成个痴呆<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我就这么站在地上琢磨<span><span>，</span></span>甚至想过以头抢地<span><span>。</span></span>终于<span><span>，</span></span>我决定了<span><span>，</span></span>还是出去死<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可我这一只脚刚伸出茅草屋<span><span>，</span></span>便瞧见了那个踏着台阶走上来的人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>闵荀…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我惊呆了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这不是下令诛我九族的小皇帝么<span><span>？</span></span>他这么快就找到这儿来了<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>真是踏破铁鞋无觅处<span><span>，</span></span>得来全不费工夫<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我即刻束手就擒<span><span>，</span></span>迫不及待地把脖子递了上去<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你杀了我吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>小皇帝微微蹙眉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>害…就地正法这么仓促也确实不符合人间事事烦琐的程序<span><span>。</span></span>于是我缩回脖子<span><span>，</span></span>乖乖伸出两只手腕<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>给我铐回去吧<span><span>，</span></span>明天送我归西<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说完<span><span>，</span></span>我有点儿担心小皇帝误会我拖延时间<span><span>，</span></span>于是又补了一句<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>当然<span><span>，</span></span>今天行刑也不是不可以<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>小皇帝那眉毛拧得更紧了<span><span>，</span></span>他盯着我<span><span>，</span></span>语气不容置疑<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你恨我<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我摆了摆手<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你想多了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>小皇帝咬了下牙<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可我…诛了你九族<span><span>。</span></span>你该恨我的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>算了<span><span>，</span></span>多说无益<span><span>。</span></span>他说恨就恨吧<span><span>。</span></span>这些都不重要<span><span>，</span></span>重要的是我啥时候能死<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>咱们什么时候走<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>去哪儿<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 小皇帝装傻充愣<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>回去…行刑…<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我试着提示<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>小皇帝一脸无语<span><span>，</span></span>我听得出他强压着怒火<span><span>，</span></span>对我解释道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>昨日<span><span>，</span></span>是我救你出来<span><span>，</span></span>又为何要再带你回去<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哈…<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我愣住了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>小皇帝说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你放心<span><span>，</span></span>已经偷梁换柱<span><span>，</span></span>没人知道你还活着<span><span>。</span></span>过两年等事情淡了<span><span>，</span></span>我给你换一个新的身份<span><span>，</span></span>你就可以…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>且慢…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>不等他说完<span><span>，</span></span>我便打断了他<span><span>，</span></span>缓缓伸出颤抖的手<span><span>，</span></span>不可置信得看着他<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你的意思是说…诛我九族…偏偏落下我一个<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>其实我想说的是…难道就差我一个了么<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>小皇帝看着我<span><span>，</span></span>试图解释<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>颂儿…你父兄造反之事不平<span><span>，</span></span>难以平朝堂<span><span>，</span></span>难以平民愤<span><span>。</span></span>可我知道<span><span>，</span></span>这些与你都没有关系…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你怎么知道就没有关系<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我蹙眉看着小皇帝<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这事我也有参与<span><span>。</span></span>确切来说…是我出的主意<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>小皇帝一怔<span><span>，</span></span>眼角颤了一下<span><span>，</span></span>身子一晃<span><span>，</span></span>差点站不稳<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>颂儿…你…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他无语<span><span>，</span></span>我更无语<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>明明我已经把证据摆得好好的了<span><span>，</span></span>可这凡人小皇帝怎么就活生生看不见呢<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>算了<span><span>，</span></span>多说无益<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>所以我们什么时候走<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>小皇帝好像难过多于生气<span><span>。</span></span>他红着眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>眼眶里噙着泪珠儿<span><span>。</span></span>他问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>为什么要这么做<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>为什么…为了完成任务<span><span>，</span></span>顺利回到地府…但我不能说<span><span>。</span></span>看来<span><span>，</span></span>我若不能给他一个看似真实的满意答复<span><span>，</span></span>他是不肯罢休的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我正苦想<span><span>，</span></span>他忽然问<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>因为李穆禾<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>谁<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我晕头转向<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>想了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>才想起他说的那个短命少年郎<span><span>。</span></span>昔日大将军府的嫡子<span><span>，</span></span>亡于弱冠的少年将军李穆禾<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>对<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我睁大眼睛看着小皇帝<span><span>，</span></span>压着嗓子<span><span>，</span></span>冷冰冰道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>若不是先皇昏庸<span><span>，</span></span>将军府不会蒙受不白之冤<span><span>。</span></span>若不是你视若不见<span><span>，</span></span>李穆禾他不会反<span><span>！</span></span>若不是你以我作饵<span><span>，</span></span>李穆禾也就不会死<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我一连气儿得说着<span><span>，</span></span>一颗心拧巴得极其难受<span><span>。</span></span>可也就只是这凡人的肉身难受罢了<span><span>。</span></span>说实话<span><span>，</span></span>我并不难过<span><span>，</span></span>甚至有些忘记了那孩子的样貌<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那小皇帝脸色铁青<span><span>，</span></span>嘴唇颤着<span><span>，</span></span>还在解释<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我说过很多次…我没有拿你做饵…那是…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>够了<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我依旧没有让他把话说完<span><span>，</span></span>因为我觉得那都不重要<span><span>。</span></span>重要的是<span><span>，</span></span>我这凡人的躯壳如今透不过气来<span><span>，</span></span>憋得我十分难受<span><span>。</span></span>我迫不及待要离开这具肉身<span><span>，</span></span>回到地府去逍遥<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>就在这时<span><span>，</span></span>我眼尖得发现小皇帝的腰间别着一把佩剑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>对不住了<span><span>，</span></span>看来要死在你面前了<span><span>。</span></span>想着<span><span>，</span></span>我飞奔过去<span><span>，</span></span>极其迅速地抽出他的佩剑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>闵荀<span><span>，</span></span>黄泉路上<span><span>，</span></span>我等着你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>长剑横颈而过<span><span>，</span></span>我瞥见了喷涌的血溅在了小皇帝的脸上<span><span>，</span></span>瞧见了他错愕惊恐的眼神<span><span>。</span></span>我最后记住的<span><span>，</span></span>是他瞪着眼睛落泪<span><span>，</span></span>仰头痛哭<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我死在了他的怀里<span><span>。</span></span>确切来说<span><span>，</span></span>十八岁的姜叶颂死在了他的怀里<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>据闻<span><span>，</span></span>姜叶颂死前说的那句话被小皇帝一直记着<span><span>，</span></span>为了那句话<span><span>，</span></span>他心痛了整整三年<span><span>，</span></span>积郁成疾<span><span>，</span></span>直到死前<span><span>，</span></span>也无法释怀<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>天知道<span><span>，</span></span>我想说的只是表面意思<span><span>，</span></span>我只是想提示他<span><span>，</span></span>我会在黄泉路上等着他而已<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>毕竟<span><span>，</span></span>我其实是个押魂使<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>3<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>我是阴间的押魂使<span><span>，</span></span>品阶比一般鬼差要高出许多<span><span>。</span></span>除了在阎王面前<span><span>，</span></span>我也是不常笑的<span><span>。</span></span>地府之中<span><span>，</span></span>他们也都称我一声儿<span><span>「</span></span>林大人<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>地府的押魂使一共只有五个<span><span>。</span></span>有一个因为与九重天的神仙成亲<span><span>，</span></span>被带去天上了<span><span>。</span></span>有一个因为私放袅袅林的犯人被关了起来<span><span>，</span></span>还有一个因为得罪阎王<span><span>，</span></span>被调去当了孟婆<span><span>。</span></span>如今地府之中便只剩下我与檀逢两个押魂使<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>彼时<span><span>，</span></span>他看见我<span><span>，</span></span>与我激动相拥<span><span>，</span></span>涕泗横流<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>兄弟<span><span>，</span></span>你可回来了<span><span>。</span></span>你真是不知道…就剩我一个人…不…一只鬼…有多可怕…多孤独<span><span>。</span></span>每次单独去见阎王大人<span><span>，</span></span>我那是如坐针毡…如…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>行了行了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>每次听檀逢说话<span><span>，</span></span>我都觉得耳朵刺挠<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>最近地府张灯结彩<span><span>，</span></span>不是啥节日吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我故意咳嗽着<span><span>，</span></span>脸上带着微笑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>檀逢老实点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不是啥节日<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯…<span><span>」</span></span> 我故作深沉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>太隆重了<span><span>，</span></span>倒是也没必要<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>有必要的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 檀逢十分认真<span><span>。</span></span>给我又整不好意思了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我忙摆了摆手<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>也不是啥大…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你不知道<span><span>，</span></span>鬼王要回来了么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 檀逢忽然打断我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>鬼王<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我一愣<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>檀逢又点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>八百年了<span><span>，</span></span>鬼王终于云游归来<span><span>，</span></span>我地府再也不用怕那九重天了<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可是我…<span><span>」</span></span> 我伸出手指指了指自己<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我<span><span>，</span></span>地府首屈一指的押魂使林拂<span><span>，</span></span>去了那比地狱还要地狱的人间<span><span>，</span></span>卧薪尝胆一十八年<span><span>，</span></span>好不容易立功归来<span><span>。</span></span>竟跟鬼王云游归来这样的大事件撞到了一起<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>呜呼哀哉<span><span>，</span></span>何其悲惨<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但比这更悲惨的事<span><span>，</span></span>很快便出现了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>话说<span><span>，</span></span>鬼王回来以后那是相当看不惯地府近几百年来的做派<span><span>，</span></span>于是开始大规模整顿地府<span><span>。</span></span>阎王大人虽说不大乐意<span><span>，</span></span>可鬼王毕竟是当年幽冥之后<span><span>，</span></span>他也没什么资格说不<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>自那日起<span><span>，</span></span>因为不称职而被送去投胎的鬼差一拨接着一拨<span><span>，</span></span>吓得大家惶惶不可终日<span><span>。</span></span>我与檀逢忙得脚打后脑勺<span><span>，</span></span>只因鬼差少了<span><span>，</span></span>地府的活儿没人干<span><span>，</span></span>原本不属于押魂使职责范畴的事儿也堆过来不少<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>某个瞬间<span><span>，</span></span>我竟有点儿想逃回人间<span><span>，</span></span>逃回那个已经被诛了九族的丞相府<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>后来<span><span>，</span></span>我听死了的人说<span><span>，</span></span>黄泉路上<span><span>，</span></span>姜叶颂的父母兄弟还找了她许久<span><span>。</span></span>送他们往生的鬼差不忍心告诉他们真相<span><span>，</span></span>于是便说<span><span>，</span></span>她留在地府做了鬼差<span><span>，</span></span>不能再与他们同路<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他们不知道<span><span>，</span></span>我曾去送过他们的<span><span>。</span></span>我与我那被贬为孟婆的押魂使兄弟换了半晌的身份<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那个给他们舀孟婆汤的人<span><span>，</span></span>是我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>4<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>这日<span><span>，</span></span>我刚从黄泉回来<span><span>，</span></span>半个时辰后要去袅袅林同檀逢交班<span><span>。</span></span>我琢磨着先在宣琅殿打个盹儿<span><span>，</span></span>可不想<span><span>，</span></span>我刚坐在台阶上<span><span>，</span></span>屁股还没坐热<span><span>，</span></span>就感觉有什么人<span><span>，</span></span>哦不<span><span>，</span></span>有什么鬼在看着我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我猛地抬头瞧过去<span><span>，</span></span>是个穿着官服的鬼差<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那鬼差瞧着眼生<span><span>，</span></span>似是个没见过的<span><span>。</span></span>他一直盯着我<span><span>，</span></span>盯得我有些发毛<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>新来的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我冰冷的眸子直勾勾回盯着那个鬼差<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你认识我<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差拱手行礼<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>鼎鼎大名的押魂使林大人<span><span>，</span></span>谁人不知<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我不是这个意思<span><span>。</span></span>我是说你为何盯着我看<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那鬼差反问我道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人不看我<span><span>，</span></span>又怎知我在看你<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我无语地看着那鬼差<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你很无聊么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>又摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>刚送走了一只鬼<span><span>，</span></span>现在确实没什么事做<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哈<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我一阵惊讶<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>最近死的人这样少了<span><span>？</span></span>人…人的寿命变…长了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>回忆起当年我还是个普通鬼差的时候<span><span>，</span></span>那是没黑天没白天<span><span>。</span></span>哦<span><span>，</span></span>当然了<span><span>，</span></span>地府的白天也不算白天的<span><span>。</span></span>我是没黑天没黑天得卖命干活儿<span><span>。</span></span>这一年到头<span><span>，</span></span>就没有休息的时候<span><span>。</span></span>怎么如今轮到这些年轻鬼<span><span>，</span></span>就闲成了这副样子<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我正想着<span><span>，</span></span>只听鬼差淡淡道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>人的寿命再长也不过百年<span><span>，</span></span>还能长到哪里<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>听这鬼差的语气<span><span>，</span></span>多半是个新鬼<span><span>，</span></span>带着过去的记忆<span><span>，</span></span>还放不下生前的事<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>害…</p>
 <p>我叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>语重心长道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>做鬼呢<span><span>，</span></span>最忌讳放不下<span><span>。</span></span>若投胎去也就罢了<span><span>，</span></span>可而今你做了鬼差<span><span>，</span></span>还有很长的日子要过<span><span>。</span></span>等再过了千八百年<span><span>，</span></span>你就会以为<span><span>，</span></span>凡间那区区几十载<span><span>，</span></span>不过就像一场梦<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>梦…<span><span>」</span></span> 鬼差喃喃念叨着<span><span>，</span></span>一双水灵灵的眼睛望着我<span><span>，</span></span>认真问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>所以凡间的所有于你而言<span><span>，</span></span>不过是一场梦么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>凡间<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我轻轻挑眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你听说过我<span><span>，</span></span>却没人告诉你<span><span>，</span></span>我当年是个死胎<span><span>，</span></span>就出生在地府么<span><span>？</span></span>凡间那场梦<span><span>，</span></span>我做都没做过<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差依旧不错眼珠儿地看着我<span><span>，</span></span>表情极其认真<span><span>。</span></span>他说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我说的不是这个…我说的是姜叶颂<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我愣了一下<span><span>，</span></span>而后问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>连姜叶颂的事你都知道<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差没有回应<span><span>，</span></span>只是自顾自又说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我方才送走的那只鬼<span><span>，</span></span>叫闵荀<span><span>，</span></span>他不肯投胎<span><span>，</span></span>还想再见你一面<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>闵荀<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我又是一愣<span><span>，</span></span>随后问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>他要见姜叶颂<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差看着我<span><span>，</span></span>直白问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>听闻你曾答应过他<span><span>，</span></span>会在黄泉路上等他<span><span>。</span></span>为何没有去<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差的声音竟透着一丝质问<span><span>，</span></span>问得我略微又有那么一丝心虚<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我弱弱道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你也知道<span><span>，</span></span>地府的押魂使如今只剩下我与檀逢<span><span>，</span></span>每日忙都忙不过来<span><span>。</span></span>昨日又有鬼夜闯袅袅林…我昨…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>说到底<span><span>，</span></span>你终究没把他放在心上<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差忽然打断了我<span><span>，</span></span>乌青的脸色仿佛更阴沉了<span><span>。</span></span>语气沉沉<span><span>，</span></span>听着还有那么一丝丝…咬牙切齿<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我瞧着他奇怪<span><span>，</span></span>便问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你与那闵荀是认识的<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>只是方才送了他一路<span><span>，</span></span>听了些你们的故事<span><span>。</span></span>总以为你并非如此绝情<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>忽然又问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你什么时候去见见他<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我沉默片刻<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>让他好生投胎去吧<span><span>，</span></span>我不见他<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差瞪起眼睛<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>为何不见<span><span>？</span></span>他都死了<span><span>，</span></span>你也不肯见他最后一面么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这鬼好生奇怪<span><span>。</span></span>我见不见小皇帝<span><span>，</span></span>给他激动成这个样子做什么<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我狐疑地看了鬼差一眼<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>去见他一面<span><span>，</span></span>原本没什么不可以<span><span>，</span></span>我也曾打算这样做的<span><span>。</span></span>但而今他因此事滞留地府<span><span>，</span></span>便是生出执念<span><span>。</span></span>你们这些新鬼<span><span>，</span></span>总以为平了执念<span><span>，</span></span>人便可以往生<span><span>。</span></span>其实不然<span><span>，</span></span>圆满才会生出更多的欲望<span><span>，</span></span>这种欲望<span><span>，</span></span>最易炼化妖魔<span><span>，</span></span>是地府的大忌<span><span>。</span></span>所以<span><span>，</span></span>我是不会去的<span><span>。</span></span>你尽早送他去投胎吧<span><span>，</span></span>就当没见过我<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>跟这鬼差说了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>我是困意全无<span><span>。</span></span>索性提剑起身<span><span>，</span></span>打算直接去袅袅林算了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我刚转过身<span><span>，</span></span>鬼差忽然又道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>他那么爱你<span><span>，</span></span>你就如此铁石心肠么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我蹙了蹙眉<span><span>，</span></span>耳朵一动<span><span>，</span></span>仿佛都听不懂鬼话了<span><span>。</span></span>我微微回过头<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>谁和谁<span><span>？</span></span>你说小皇帝爱姜叶颂<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差初是盯着我看<span><span>，</span></span>随后轻轻点了点头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑了<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是谁告诉你小皇帝爱姜叶颂的<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>黄泉路上<span><span>，</span></span>闵荀亲口说的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>真是不靠谱<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 鬼差似乎没听清我说什么<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>他若是爱姜叶颂<span><span>，</span></span>为何要抄她满门<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差没说话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我又问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姜叶颂死后可有名分<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差欲言又止<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我淡淡道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>听闻只有个无字碑<span><span>，</span></span>孤零零立在南莱山<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差依旧没有说话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我见他一句话也说不出<span><span>，</span></span>眉头蹙着<span><span>，</span></span>仿佛受到了打击<span><span>，</span></span>一时瞧着竟有些可怜<span><span>。</span></span>于是我劝慰道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>尘世多纷扰<span><span>，</span></span>何苦谈论那些虚幻的东西<span><span>？</span></span>其实闵荀与姜叶颂如何<span><span>，</span></span>同你我又有何相干<span><span>？</span></span>你根本无须为此事烦忧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姜叶颂<span><span>，</span></span>姜叶颂…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>那鬼眉毛拧巴着<span><span>，</span></span>摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你口口声声姜叶颂<span><span>，</span></span>可那不就是你么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我眨了眨眼<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可我是林拂啊…我不过是扮演了姜叶颂罢了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>那鬼不可置信地看着我<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可终究是你走完了姜叶颂的一生<span><span>，</span></span>与闵荀相处了十几年的<span><span>，</span></span>也是你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我还是不明白…<span><span>」</span></span> 我声音一顿<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>无论如何<span><span>，</span></span>我也只是林拂而已<span><span>，</span></span>我从未当自己是过那个凡间女子<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>那鬼看着我<span><span>，</span></span>眼珠儿仿佛要掉了出来<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>所以<span><span>，</span></span>你便从未付出过真心<span><span>，</span></span>对么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我轻轻笑了<span><span>，</span></span>毫无冒犯的意思<span><span>，</span></span>而是真的发自内心觉得有趣<span><span>。</span></span>我耐心解释道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我是阎王养大的<span><span>，</span></span>阎王自入地府就被挖去心肝<span><span>。</span></span>他既没有心<span><span>，</span></span>我又何来的真心呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差盯着我<span><span>，</span></span>盯着盯着竟然笑了<span><span>。</span></span>他点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>不知是喜是悲<span><span>，</span></span>只是瞧着表情有些阴森<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>原来是这样…青出于蓝胜于蓝<span><span>，</span></span>原来你比没有心的阎王还要绝情<span><span>。</span></span>所以林大人才能成为这地府之中最出色的押魂使<span><span>，</span></span>就连袅袅林中的鬼都闻风丧胆<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差的声音渐渐变了<span><span>，</span></span>幽缓冷涩<span><span>，</span></span>我一个哆嗦<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>等等…这动静咋听着有点儿耳熟呢…</p>
 <p>来不及多回忆<span><span>，</span></span>一片黑雾之中<span><span>，</span></span>只见那鬼差一挥衣袖<span><span>，</span></span>原本的鬼差消失了<span><span>，</span></span>取而代之的<span><span>，</span></span>是一张陌生面孔<span><span>，</span></span>皮肤苍白<span><span>，</span></span>瞳孔幽深<span><span>，</span></span>细长的手指上带着一枚透着血丝的黄玉扳指<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他苍白的手指缓缓转动着扳指<span><span>，</span></span>盯着我<span><span>，</span></span>轻弯了弯唇角<span><span>，</span></span>幽幽说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>有押魂使如此<span><span>，</span></span>真乃地府之幸<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你…<span><span>」</span></span> 我愣着愣着<span><span>，</span></span>瞧着那黄玉<span><span>，</span></span>再琢磨琢磨这耳熟的声音…忽然反应过来<span><span>，</span></span>即刻拱手俯身<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>鬼王大人<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>靠<span><span>！</span></span>吓死我了<span><span>！</span></span>鬼王这么喜欢捉弄人的么<span><span>？</span></span>还是说…考核这么突然就开始…啊不<span><span>，</span></span>就结束了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>？</span></span><span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼王声音透着寒气<span><span>，</span></span>似乎刚从寒冰地狱里爬出来<span><span>，</span></span>每一个字都结着冰碴<span><span>。</span></span>他冷冷笑道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>林拂<span><span>，</span></span>人世间嗔痴怨念<span><span>，</span></span>你既都已抛却彻底<span><span>，</span></span>留在地府不免可惜<span><span>。</span></span>自今日起<span><span>，</span></span>便由你带着三号牢房的那些鬼<span><span>，</span></span>去阳间办差吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>三…三号牢房…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我吭哧着<span><span>，</span></span>剩下半句话还没挤出来<span><span>，</span></span>鬼王已经消失不见了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我…我是又要回地面上去了么…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>站在袅袅林外<span><span>，</span></span>我依旧不可置信<span><span>，</span></span>把此事说与檀逢<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>檀逢怜悯地瞧着我<span><span>，</span></span>拍了拍我的肩膀<span><span>，</span></span>叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>只说了两个字<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>节哀…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>5<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>我回到凡间的第一个案子就有点棘手<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>话说那雪桑谷中有只老鬼撒泼打滚<span><span>，</span></span>就是不肯跟鬼差走<span><span>。</span></span>每每鬼差出现<span><span>，</span></span>他总是能神奇躲开<span><span>。</span></span>一来二去<span><span>，</span></span>折腾了十年有余<span><span>，</span></span>抓他的鬼差精疲力竭<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>说来此事为何难缠<span><span>，</span></span>还有一点重要原因<span><span>。</span></span>听闻那鬼死后几年<span><span>，</span></span>他那运簿无故被烧<span><span>，</span></span>只剩下残卷<span><span>。</span></span>地府为了盖住这事儿<span><span>，</span></span>不敢声张<span><span>。</span></span>你说对他下死手吧<span><span>，</span></span>这鬼的运簿已经烧了<span><span>，</span></span>严格意义上来说他就没有生前的记载<span><span>，</span></span>也就无法证明他是由人变成了鬼<span><span>。</span></span>可若他不是由人变成的鬼<span><span>，</span></span>那地府就没那个权限去抓他<span><span>。</span></span>但你说不抓他吧<span><span>，</span></span>大家心里又都清清楚楚<span><span>，</span></span>这老鬼的确就是个死人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这鬼才逻辑<span><span>，</span></span>困扰了地府足足十几年<span><span>。</span></span>直到近来鬼王肃查地府<span><span>，</span></span>办案的鬼差又将此事报了上去<span><span>，</span></span>于是便落到了三号牢房手里<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>如今<span><span>，</span></span>我作为三号牢房的大哥<span><span>，</span></span>哦不<span><span>，</span></span>大姐<span><span>，</span></span>理所应当前往雪桑谷会会那只老鬼<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>临走前<span><span>，</span></span>阎王大人怕我坏事<span><span>，</span></span>再三嘱咐道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>只可智取<span><span>，</span></span>不可力敌<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>带着满满自信甚至是微微自满<span><span>，</span></span>我又回到了地面上<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>说起这雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>多年前我曾经来过的<span><span>。</span></span>以姜叶颂的身份在谷中学了两年医术<span><span>。</span></span>昔日<span><span>，</span></span>雪桑谷的当家还是莫连声<span><span>，</span></span>如今早就换成了他儿子莫英<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>当莫英见到我的时候<span><span>，</span></span>吓了一大跳<span><span>。</span></span>眼珠儿鼓着<span><span>，</span></span>手指颤着<span><span>，</span></span>嘴里阿巴阿巴个不停<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>而我云淡风轻<span><span>，</span></span>相当有风骨地拱了拱手<span><span>，</span></span>淡淡然自报家门<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>在下昆仑林拂<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>此番三号牢房跟我上来的鬼名为苏温<span><span>，</span></span>此时也拱了拱手<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>在下昆仑苏温<span><span>。</span></span>我与师姐此番前来<span><span>，</span></span>希望不会打扰到雪桑谷<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鉴于雪桑谷那只鬼无比狡猾奸诈<span><span>，</span></span>为了让他放松警惕<span><span>，</span></span>我决定给我和苏温捏个人间身份<span><span>。</span></span>而在人间之所以冒认昆仑的人<span><span>，</span></span>一来因为那地方山高水远<span><span>，</span></span>鲜与外界来往<span><span>，</span></span>露馅儿比较慢<span><span>。</span></span>二来因为昆仑在地面上很吃得开<span><span>，</span></span>极少有人敢质疑<span><span>，</span></span>更别说插手昆仑的事<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>此时莫英终于回过神来<span><span>，</span></span>拱了拱手<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>在下雪桑谷莫英<span><span>，</span></span>有失远迎<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英又看了我一眼<span><span>，</span></span>而后吩咐谷中弟子带我们去安排好的厢房<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>路过东厢<span><span>，</span></span>我隐约好似闻着一股松木香<span><span>。</span></span>我蹙了蹙眉<span><span>，</span></span>侧头问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>雪桑谷除了我们<span><span>，</span></span>还有别的客人<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>那送我们去厢房的少年点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>而后微微愣了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>您怎么知道的<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我又瞥了那东厢房一眼<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是归玉城的玉松香<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>少年又点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>的确<span><span>，</span></span>不日前<span><span>，</span></span>归玉城来了两位公子<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>归玉城的人无故不出焚京渡<span><span>，</span></span>此番前来<span><span>，</span></span>难道和我们一样<span><span>，</span></span>也是为了讨教医术<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>少年欲言又止<span><span>，</span></span>好似有些事说不出口<span><span>，</span></span>沉默了数秒<span><span>，</span></span>才道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>确不是为了医术前来<span><span>，</span></span>只是谷中发生了些事情<span><span>，</span></span>请归玉城的公子过来帮忙<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着功夫<span><span>，</span></span>已经走到了房间门口<span><span>。</span></span>我也不好再作追问<span><span>，</span></span>只得作罢<span><span>。</span></span>将我们送到房间后<span><span>，</span></span>少年离开了<span><span>。</span></span>苏温一直盯着我<span><span>，</span></span>盯了好一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>忽然问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>你怎么会知道归玉城的事<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大惊小怪<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我把剑放到了书案上<span><span>，</span></span>边倒了一盏谷里新送来的热茶<span><span>，</span></span>边说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>多年前<span><span>，</span></span>我在人间有任务<span><span>，</span></span>曾在这谷中呆过几年<span><span>，</span></span>那时候认识了归玉城的几个少年<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>我又想了想<span><span>，</span></span>改口道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>或许<span><span>，</span></span>现在也不能说是少年了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那你也认识莫谷主<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我<span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>」</span></span>了一声儿<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>当时他也就十五六岁<span><span>，</span></span>身子孱弱<span><span>、</span></span>也没什么天份<span><span>，</span></span>我从未想过<span><span>，</span></span>他会成为雪桑谷未来的谷主<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温微微蹙了蹙眉<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可是听闻雪桑谷莫英的医术很是高超<span><span>，</span></span>与昆仑薛冷<span><span>、</span></span>归玉城秦一迟并称北岭三绝<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那我就不知道了<span><span>。</span></span>也许后来又有了什么机缘也说不定<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我说着<span><span>，</span></span>抿了口茶<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>好死不死<span><span>，</span></span>听苏温这鬼小子一说<span><span>，</span></span>我就回忆起昔日的一些片段来<span><span>。</span></span>说来也是荣幸<span><span>，</span></span>人间所谓的北岭三绝<span><span>，</span></span>我竟认识两个<span><span>。</span></span>那归玉城的秦一迟当年的确厉害<span><span>，</span></span>不过是个脾气暴躁的主儿<span><span>，</span></span>得理不饶人<span><span>、</span></span>无理辩三分<span><span>，</span></span>撒泼打混不在话下<span><span>。</span></span>可就这么两个最不像当家人的人最后成了当家<span><span>，</span></span>反而当年最清朗澄明的少年<span><span>，</span></span>早早见了阎王<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我时常怀疑<span><span>，</span></span>录命司写人运簿的时候也是胡乱下笔<span><span>，</span></span>敷衍了事<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>见我失神<span><span>，</span></span>苏温伸出手在我眼前晃了晃<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>那我们现在怎么办<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我们不能轻举妄动<span><span>。</span></span>那归玉城的人会些法术<span><span>，</span></span>虽不及昆仑厉害<span><span>，</span></span>可也容易被他们识破<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温若有所思得点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>许久<span><span>，</span></span>忽然倒吸了口气<span><span>，</span></span>一脸懵然看着我<span><span>，</span></span>缓缓道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不对啊…大人<span><span>，</span></span>我们是地府的差<span><span>，</span></span>又不是作恶的鬼<span><span>。</span></span>我们怕什么啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我哼了一声<span><span>，</span></span>随手给苏温倒上了茶<span><span>，</span></span>耐心讲道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>谁管你什么差不差<span><span>，</span></span>地府不地府<span><span>。</span></span>你不了解人这种东西<span><span>。</span></span>人呢<span><span>，</span></span>对自己不了解的东西有一种深深的恐惧<span><span>。</span></span>在他们心中<span><span>，</span></span>世间万事万物<span><span>，</span></span>你不寻常便是异类<span><span>，</span></span>没什么道理可讲<span><span>。</span></span>这是一种近乎变态的执念<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温被我的学识深深折服<span><span>，</span></span>缓缓点了点头<span><span>。</span></span>忽然眼里闪过一丝精光<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>那你说<span><span>，</span></span>归玉城此番受邀前来和他们的法术有没有关系<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你说那只老鬼<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我抬眼看向苏温<span><span>，</span></span>压着嗓子问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温<span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>」</span></span>了一声儿<span><span>，</span></span>而后又露出一抹疑惑神色<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可我听此前来过雪桑谷的鬼差说<span><span>，</span></span>那老鬼虽说狡猾<span><span>，</span></span>可平日还算老实<span><span>，</span></span>没在人间惹出什么祸事<span><span>。</span></span>如果是这样的话<span><span>，</span></span>雪桑谷是怎么发现他的<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我也想不出个所以然<span><span>，</span></span>只得说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>无论如何…我们都需得先找到老鬼再说<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>其实我有个事一直也想不明白<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>他死了这么多年都不离开雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>是为了什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>的确<span><span>，</span></span>老鬼既有这本事<span><span>，</span></span>在雪桑谷范围内转悠都能躲过鬼差<span><span>。</span></span>若是出了雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>恐怕鬼差几辈子也逮不住他了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不离开雪桑谷无非两种情况<span><span>。</span></span>一<span><span>，</span></span>他不愿意走<span><span>，</span></span>二<span><span>，</span></span>他走不了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我淡定说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>几个回合下来<span><span>，</span></span>没啥见识的苏温对我已是五体投地<span><span>。</span></span>围着我<span><span>，</span></span>问了好些雪桑谷当年的情况<span><span>。</span></span>入了夜<span><span>，</span></span>我好不容易打发了他<span><span>，</span></span>刚刚躺在榻上<span><span>，</span></span>眼睛还未闭紧<span><span>，</span></span>便听见门外传来一阵尖叫<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我腾然起身<span><span>，</span></span>抓起案上的长剑<span><span>，</span></span>疾步走了出去<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>来人啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 有人大喊<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>循着声音<span><span>，</span></span>我很快赶到东厢<span><span>，</span></span>归玉城两个小公子住的房间门是大开着的<span><span>。</span></span>门边躺着个穿着雪桑谷衣服的少年<span><span>，</span></span>脸色青白<span><span>，</span></span>估计是被吓昏了过去<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一个少年几乎与我同步赶到<span><span>，</span></span>瞧着穿着应是归玉城的人<span><span>。</span></span>他还未跨进门去<span><span>，</span></span>已是目瞪口呆<span><span>。</span></span>只见一跟他穿着同样衣服的少年倒在地上<span><span>，</span></span>喉咙已经被划破<span><span>，</span></span>可是周围一滴血也没有<span><span>，</span></span>再看那尸体<span><span>，</span></span>已经成了一具干尸<span><span>。</span></span>少年面容枯槁<span><span>，</span></span>眼睛死死瞪着<span><span>，</span></span>我一只鬼瞧着都害怕<span><span>，</span></span>可别说那个第一个发现的凡人少年了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我在此看着<span><span>，</span></span>你快去叫人<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我对那归玉城的少年说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>少年也没什么防范心<span><span>，</span></span>对我匆忙拱了拱手<span><span>，</span></span>便提剑寻人去了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>少年走了<span><span>，</span></span>我眯了眯眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>还记得是怎么死的么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>不远处站着的<span><span>，</span></span>那惨死的少年看了一眼倒在地上的自己的肉身<span><span>，</span></span>摇了摇头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>害…人刚死<span><span>，</span></span>总是很懵<span><span>。</span></span>别说你问他是怎么死的<span><span>，</span></span>你就问他是谁<span><span>，</span></span>他可能都答不上来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你是谁<span><span>？</span></span>为什么可以看见我<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 惨死鬼看着我<span><span>，</span></span>不等我回答<span><span>，</span></span>便又问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>鬼差<span><span>？</span></span>你是鬼差<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我是地府的差<span><span>，</span></span>但不是来带你走的鬼差<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我简短回答了他<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼蹙着眉<span><span>，</span></span>没有说话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没有多长时间了<span><span>，</span></span>来带你的鬼差马上就会到<span><span>。</span></span>你不想知道自己是怎么死的么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我能做什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 惨死鬼问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还记得死前做过什么么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼看着躺在地上的肉身<span><span>，</span></span>道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我从外面回来…找谷里的人要了壶茶<span><span>。</span></span>然后坐在桌前等…再然后…我就倒在这儿了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>虽说他这描述基本省略了最关键的部分<span><span>。</span></span>不过行吧<span><span>，</span></span>聊胜于无<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我觉得我是中邪了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 惨死鬼忽然说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>邪<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我眉毛一拧<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>什么意思<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>在我之前<span><span>，</span></span>这里已经接连死了几个人<span><span>，</span></span>怀疑有鬼魅作祟<span><span>。</span></span>莫谷主才找上我们归玉城的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>鬼魅<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我盯着那惨死鬼<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>为什么说是鬼魅<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>因为他们死状凄惨诡异<span><span>，</span></span>且出奇地一致<span><span>，</span></span>不像是人为<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>就像你这样的死法<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼点了点头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>还不等我再说什么<span><span>，</span></span>惨死鬼忽然问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>既不是来带我走的<span><span>，</span></span>地府的差<span><span>，</span></span>为何无缘无故出现在这里<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你既死了<span><span>，</span></span>我也不瞒你<span><span>。</span></span>地府在追一只鬼<span><span>，</span></span>就在这雪桑谷中<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼眼睛一瞪<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>岂不就是我们在找的那个<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不对<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那只鬼死了有年头了<span><span>，</span></span>都没害过人<span><span>。</span></span>不可能突然作乱的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>那惨死鬼好似有些不服气<span><span>，</span></span>此时脸色更加苍白了<span><span>。</span></span>他盯着我道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那可是鬼<span><span>，</span></span>你怎能以常人的心态去看一只鬼呢<span><span>？</span></span>还有<span><span>，</span></span>你们地府究竟是做什么的<span><span>？</span></span>竟然放任死了多年的鬼为祸人间<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我冷冷看着那惨死鬼<span><span>，</span></span>一字一字道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你已经是一只鬼了<span><span>。</span></span>这样讲自己的同族<span><span>，</span></span>恐怕不太好<span><span>。</span></span>还有<span><span>，</span></span>这世上<span><span>，</span></span>有笨鬼<span><span>，</span></span>就有聪明鬼<span><span>，</span></span>而这些聪明鬼中还有一些尤其狡猾<span><span>。</span></span>地府也不是万能的<span><span>，</span></span>总有那么几只会暂时脱离掌控<span><span>，</span></span>你应该理解<span><span>，</span></span>毕竟我们也在尽力抓捕<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼没有再争白<span><span>，</span></span>只是淡淡道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你应该是地府里最能狡辩的鬼了吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我冷笑了一下<span><span>，</span></span>拱了拱手<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>承让承让<span><span>，</span></span>押魂使林拂<span><span>，</span></span>敢问兄台大名<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼拱了拱手<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>归玉城秦一行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>秦一行<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我愣了一下<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>秦一迟是你什么人<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼沉默片刻<span><span>，</span></span>才道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是家兄<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>同胞兄弟<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼点了点头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着眼前死了都站得挺直的秦一行<span><span>，</span></span>还真瞧出些秦一迟的影子<span><span>。</span></span>只是似乎两兄弟的个性全然不同<span><span>，</span></span>至少目前瞧着是这样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我死了<span><span>，</span></span>我哥恐怕会与雪桑谷没完没了<span><span>。</span></span>若是可以<span><span>，</span></span>烦劳姑娘帮我带句话<span><span>，</span></span>就说此番惨死只因我法术不精<span><span>，</span></span>归玉城莫与雪桑谷为难<span><span>。</span></span>若非如此<span><span>，</span></span>我秦一行死不瞑目<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你觉得你哥秦一迟会听我的<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我可不是不乐意帮他带话<span><span>。</span></span>只是一来给鬼带话等于自报家门<span><span>，</span></span>二来是秦一迟年少时便十分执拗<span><span>，</span></span>最是听不进劝说<span><span>，</span></span>我便是说了也没什么用<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼没说话<span><span>，</span></span>我便又说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不过<span><span>，</span></span>我可以帮你从中斡旋些<span><span>，</span></span>免得你哥做出什么出格的事<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>多谢<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 惨死鬼点了点头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>别忙着谢我<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我缓缓问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>先告诉我你们归玉城都查出什么来了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>雪桑谷从两个月前开始有人离奇身亡<span><span>。</span></span>喉咙被划破<span><span>，</span></span>周身的血被吸干<span><span>。</span></span>可血去了哪里<span><span>，</span></span>始终没人知道<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>所以你们觉得是鬼魅妖邪作祟<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>惨死鬼点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>梵音铃果然查出谷中有鬼<span><span>，</span></span>只可惜<span><span>，</span></span>我到现在也没见过它的样子<span><span>。</span></span>如今看来<span><span>，</span></span>应该就是地府找的那只<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我刚一张嘴<span><span>，</span></span>身后忽然传来一群人的脚步声<span><span>，</span></span>不多时<span><span>，</span></span>一帮人嗡得一起出现了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>眼前景象给他们一个一个吓得不轻<span><span>。</span></span>莫英此时脸上毫无血色<span><span>，</span></span>比那躺在地上的惨死鬼也差不了多少<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那鬼…鬼…鬼又来了<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫英身边的少年指着惨死鬼的尸体口中念念有词<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英咬了咬牙<span><span>，</span></span>对身侧归玉城的少年道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是我雪桑谷连累了秦公子<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>归玉城的少年蹙眉道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我已送信回归玉城<span><span>，</span></span>请人来接我师兄的尸骨<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看了站在不远处的惨死鬼一眼<span><span>，</span></span>对莫英拱手<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>如果有什么需要我师姐弟帮忙的地方<span><span>，</span></span>尽管开口<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英看着我<span><span>，</span></span>叹息道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>现今的确有件棘手的事烦请二位帮忙<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我瞥了一眼姗姗来迟的苏温<span><span>，</span></span>对莫英点了下头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>乐意效劳<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>6<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>暂时安顿好了惨死鬼的尸体<span><span>，</span></span>时候已经不早了<span><span>。</span></span>我与莫英约好了明日一早再行商讨<span><span>，</span></span>便回了房间<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>带惨死鬼走的鬼差来之前<span><span>，</span></span>我又和惨死鬼打听了些事<span><span>，</span></span>并再三允诺尽力帮着从中斡旋些<span><span>。</span></span>惨死鬼走了<span><span>，</span></span>我躺在榻上<span><span>，</span></span>睁眼等到了天明<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>天亮后<span><span>，</span></span>我简单梳洗了一下<span><span>，</span></span>提着剑敲响了苏温的门<span><span>。</span></span>我俩到正堂时莫英<span><span>、</span></span>归玉城的那个少年已经在那儿等着了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>在下昆仑林拂<span><span>，</span></span>这是我师弟苏温<span><span>。</span></span>还未请教公子大名<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我对归玉城少年拱了拱手<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>归玉城少年拱手<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>归玉城白隐<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>白公子<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我微微颔首<span><span>，</span></span>随后坐了下来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>就像没听过那惨死鬼讲过一般<span><span>，</span></span>我又听莫英说了一遍近两个月来雪桑谷的遭遇<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一番听罢<span><span>，</span></span>白隐叹了口气<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>师兄的归魂阵曾让那鬼现过一次身<span><span>。</span></span>可惜那次让他跑了<span><span>，</span></span>否则…师兄也就不会…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温眼睛一斜<span><span>，</span></span>一张嘴就没好话<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>时也命也<span><span>，</span></span>没什么可惜不可惜<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>白隐微微一愣<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我悄悄瞪了苏温一眼<span><span>，</span></span>忙岔开话题问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那鬼什么样子<span><span>，</span></span>你还记得么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>白隐回忆了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>形容道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>二十来岁的样子…身材瘦削…长得…<span><span>」</span></span> 说着<span><span>，</span></span>忽然看向莫英<span><span>，</span></span>缓声说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>长得与莫谷主倒是有几分相似<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫英蹙了蹙眉<span><span>，</span></span>似是若有所思<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我盯着莫英瞧了许久<span><span>，</span></span>回忆了一下鬼差呈上来的画像<span><span>。</span></span>别说<span><span>，</span></span>貌似还真有几分相像<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英若有所思<span><span>，</span></span>沉默许久忽然问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>白公子<span><span>，</span></span>你说的相像…究竟是相像…还是…一模一样<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>这…<span><span>」</span></span> 白隐蹙了蹙眉<span><span>，</span></span>摇头道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>只是隐约瞧见相似<span><span>，</span></span>你让我回想<span><span>，</span></span>画面竟不真切了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英喉咙一哽<span><span>，</span></span>没再说话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>害…我怎么给忘了<span><span>。</span></span>昔日这莫英还有个双生弟弟名为莫琼的<span><span>。</span></span>论天资<span><span>，</span></span>那莫琼比莫英高出百倍<span><span>，</span></span>若非是因为早亡<span><span>，</span></span>恐怕北岭三绝的医绝也轮不到莫英<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>此时<span><span>，</span></span>莫英神色有些古怪<span><span>，</span></span>微微垂着脑袋不知在想些什么<span><span>。</span></span>想必他想的事定与那个莫琼有关<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>待用过早膳<span><span>，</span></span>我与苏温找了时间单独去了莫英处拜访<span><span>。</span></span>遍寻他不见<span><span>，</span></span>听谷中的弟子说<span><span>，</span></span>他这个时间应该在莫家的祠堂<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温法力还不到时候<span><span>，</span></span>莫家的祠堂有高人做过法<span><span>，</span></span>他近不了身<span><span>。</span></span>于是我便只能只身前往<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>正巧在祠堂门口遇见莫英<span><span>，</span></span>他便邀我一同进去<span><span>。</span></span>那莫家的祠堂朴素简单<span><span>，</span></span>四排牌位前是长明的烛火随着偶尔钻进的风轻轻鼓动<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我也象征性地拜了拜<span><span>，</span></span>便站在一边仔仔细细瞧着那些排位<span><span>，</span></span>想着其中或多或少<span><span>，</span></span>我许在地府见过也说不定<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>就在这时候<span><span>，</span></span>我眼神一聚<span><span>，</span></span>便瞥见了莫琼的牌位<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫琼…<span><span>」</span></span> 我轻声念着<span><span>，</span></span>假装不知<span><span>，</span></span>试探道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>看着应是莫谷主的兄弟<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是家弟<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我假装吃惊<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>辛丑年腊月十八<span><span>？</span></span>七年前<span><span>，</span></span>令弟还很年轻啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>看着那牌位苦笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是啊<span><span>，</span></span>十九岁…永远的十九岁<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>冒昧问一句<span><span>，</span></span>令弟是怎么死的<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这个问题<span><span>，</span></span>其实是有些私心的<span><span>。</span></span>昔日在雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>我的确与莫英走动得更多<span><span>，</span></span>但我对莫琼一直有种不一样的好奇心<span><span>。</span></span>他天资极高<span><span>，</span></span>但寡言少语<span><span>，</span></span>与莫英活泼的性格正好相反<span><span>，</span></span>与谷中众人也并不如莫英那般亲近<span><span>。</span></span>可瞧着他<span><span>，</span></span>总让我想起记忆里的某个人<span><span>，</span></span>即便不愿意去回忆<span><span>，</span></span>但影子终究就在那儿<span><span>，</span></span>深深埋于心底<span><span>，</span></span>一刻不曾消失<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>听了我的问题<span><span>，</span></span>莫英也毫不避讳<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>病故<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英说着<span><span>，</span></span>忽然咳嗽起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>害…我怎么又忘了<span><span>，</span></span>莫英这小子打小就是个病秧子<span><span>。</span></span>此前端端正正瞧着好模好样的<span><span>，</span></span>如今受了些风<span><span>，</span></span>再一激动<span><span>，</span></span>咳咳嗽嗽的<span><span>，</span></span>瞧着又有少时那弱不禁风的模样了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我把披风解下来披在了他身上<span><span>。</span></span>他微微一愣<span><span>，</span></span>忽然抬眼盯着我<span><span>，</span></span>吓我一大跳<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>别受凉<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我尴尬又不失礼貌地拍了拍他的后背<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英看着我<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姑娘真的很像我一位故人<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我喉咙那么一紧<span><span>，</span></span>眼珠儿那么一顿<span><span>，</span></span>嘴上却是淡淡道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怪不得第一次见面时<span><span>，</span></span>莫谷主神色有些异常<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>少时的朋友<span><span>，</span></span>也曾像姑娘这样<span><span>，</span></span>给我披上过披风<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>等等…我啥时候给莫英披过披风…</p>
 <p>不等我回忆翻涌<span><span>，</span></span>莫英又道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>明明是个十五岁的小姑娘<span><span>，</span></span>活出了久经风霜的将军气势…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span><span>，</span></span>似乎嘴角微微扬起<span><span>，</span></span>摇了摇头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>别说<span><span>，</span></span>这莫英眼神儿真挺好使<span><span>。</span></span>当年我做押魂使之前<span><span>，</span></span>的确替地府上过几年战场<span><span>，</span></span>差点被收编进了鬼卫<span><span>。</span></span>然我实在厌烦那些打打杀杀<span><span>，</span></span>长品阶损修为的破烂差事<span><span>。</span></span>更何况如今地府与九重天修好<span><span>，</span></span>几百年来已是战事寥寥<span><span>。</span></span>于是我便请愿做了押魂使<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但是等等…眼神儿好归眼神儿好<span><span>。</span></span>我到底什么时候给莫英这小子披过披风<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我是心里一团乱<span><span>，</span></span>还不敢开口问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我轻声叹了口气<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>盖过我这一声叹息的<span><span>，</span></span>是莫英的叹息声<span><span>。</span></span>他缓缓说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>一转眼<span><span>，</span></span>已经这么多年了<span><span>。</span></span>他们都不在了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>他们<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我又开始假装听不懂<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姑娘身在昆仑<span><span>，</span></span>许是没听说过多年前的两桩谋反大案<span><span>。</span></span>一是大将军府通敌叛国<span><span>，</span></span>二是庆德政变<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我没说话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英叹了口气<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>庆德元年<span><span>，</span></span>昔日大将军府嫡子李穆禾联合桓王谋反<span><span>，</span></span>势如破竹<span><span>，</span></span>攻入帝京后却落入圈套<span><span>，</span></span>最终功败垂成<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我依旧没有说话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英继续说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>李穆禾<span><span>，</span></span>当年是和她一起来的<span><span>。</span></span>他比我们中的任何一个都要优秀<span><span>。</span></span>可惜<span><span>，</span></span>死得最早的也是他<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我还是没有说话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>抱歉…不该跟你说这些<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫英好像忽然回过神来<span><span>，</span></span>对我轻轻笑了一下<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没关系<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>逝者已矣<span><span>，</span></span>人还是要向前看<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>此时话题已经偏了<span><span>，</span></span>我看了一眼外面<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不如我们先出去再说<span><span>。</span></span>打扰先祖<span><span>，</span></span>心中实在有愧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我与莫英离开祠堂后<span><span>，</span></span>他便带我去了书房<span><span>。</span></span>我知道他应该是有什么话要说<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>莫英客套道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>此番昆仑本是来同雪桑谷探讨医术<span><span>，</span></span>可惜谷中出了这种事<span><span>。</span></span>恐怕不能如约了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>无碍<span><span>，</span></span>死者事大<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我说罢<span><span>，</span></span>拉回话题道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>对了<span><span>，</span></span>刚才说到令弟是病故<span><span>。</span></span>究竟是什么顽疾<span><span>，</span></span>连雪桑谷也治不好<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>是诅咒<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫英蹙了蹙眉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>诅咒<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我假装很吃惊<span><span>，</span></span>其实内心毫无波澜<span><span>，</span></span>甚至有一丝丝想笑<span><span>。</span></span>凡人总是动不动把一些无法解释的事怪到鬼神和诅咒的头上<span><span>，</span></span>其实哪有那么多灵验的诅咒<span><span>？</span></span>真正的鬼神都忙得很<span><span>，</span></span>没有那瞎功夫去诅咒一个凡胎肉身<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英叹息道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>听闻莫家祖上有位将军<span><span>，</span></span>背弃故国换得了至高荣耀<span><span>。</span></span>然因梦魇缠身最终选择来雪桑谷隐居<span><span>。</span></span>可自那时候开始<span><span>，</span></span>莫家的人就像是受到了诅咒<span><span>，</span></span>世世代代顽疾缠身<span><span>，</span></span>药石无医<span><span>。</span></span>我的叔叔和我的弟弟都亡于弱冠<span><span>。</span></span>我父亲虽没那样短命<span><span>，</span></span>却也活不过不惑<span><span>。</span></span>医人者不能自医<span><span>，</span></span>可能就是我雪桑谷世世代代的命运<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英的眼里透着落寞<span><span>，</span></span>许久都没有再说话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>再一开口<span><span>，</span></span>又是一阵咳嗽<span><span>。</span></span>初是轻微<span><span>，</span></span>渐渐愈发剧烈起来<span><span>，</span></span>脸色青白<span><span>，</span></span>肩膀也微微颤动着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫谷主…你还好么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我蹙眉问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英摆了摆手<span><span>，</span></span>许久<span><span>，</span></span>气息渐渐平稳了<span><span>，</span></span>才又道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>恐怕我也没有多久好活了<span><span>。</span></span>所以…这次的事一定要拜托昆仑<span><span>，</span></span>拜托二位…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>话没说完<span><span>，</span></span>又是一阵重咳<span><span>。</span></span>我瞧着他那模样<span><span>，</span></span>都跟着难受<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>要我昆仑帮忙不是不可以<span><span>。</span></span>只是莫谷主需要说些实话才行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着莫英的眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>沉沉说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英眼角一动<span><span>，</span></span>没说话<span><span>，</span></span>可我瞧着<span><span>，</span></span>他也大概知道了我想要问什么<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>为什么你觉得那只鬼会和你长得一模一样<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英一阵沉默<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你觉得那只鬼是令弟莫琼<span><span>？</span></span>为什么这么觉得<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我追问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英喉咙明显一哽<span><span>，</span></span>他缓缓抬眼看着我<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>因为他生前一直在研究破解诅咒的方法<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么方法<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我怔然看着莫英<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不知道<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫英摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>但是我弟弟死之前那几年一直神神秘秘的<span><span>，</span></span>还说什么终于找到了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你是说那些人的死…和破除诅咒的方法有关<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英叹了口气<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我不知道<span><span>。</span></span>可是我弟弟他…并非滥杀之人<span><span>，</span></span>除非他有什么不得已的理由<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>虽然莫英嘴上没那么说<span><span>，</span></span>但心中似乎已经认定那鬼就是莫琼<span><span>。</span></span>我是真想告诉他<span><span>，</span></span>那鬼不是莫琼<span><span>，</span></span>那只老鬼死于十多年前<span><span>，</span></span>彼时<span><span>，</span></span>那莫琼还好端端活在世上<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可是我不能说<span><span>，</span></span>只能任由莫英胡思乱想<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>说来是十分无语<span><span>。</span></span>话说这老鬼的运簿被烧<span><span>，</span></span>当年办案的鬼差也迷迷糊糊<span><span>，</span></span>竟忘了这鬼的名字和来历<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>地府虽已着手去查<span><span>，</span></span>但动作着实是慢<span><span>。</span></span>毕竟是要往上界录命司去找<span><span>，</span></span>多多少少吃力了些<span><span>。</span></span>彼时<span><span>，</span></span>因为得了令<span><span>，</span></span>我与苏温便先上来了<span><span>，</span></span>随时等着地府的消息<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>想着<span><span>，</span></span>我头又疼了起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>按道理说<span><span>，</span></span>那鬼既长得同莫英有几分相似<span><span>，</span></span>便极有可能是他的血亲<span><span>。</span></span>按着年头来看<span><span>，</span></span>多半是个长辈<span><span>。</span></span>想着<span><span>，</span></span>我试着问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>多嘴问一句<span><span>，</span></span>近二十年间除了令弟<span><span>，</span></span>莫谷主还有亲人离世么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英想了想<span><span>，</span></span>回道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>家父在五年前病故<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 说罢<span><span>，</span></span>又补充道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还有我小叔叔<span><span>。</span></span>大概死了快二十年了<span><span>，</span></span>那时候我年纪还小<span><span>，</span></span>记得不太真切<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>小叔叔…<span><span>」</span></span> 我心下忽然狂喜<span><span>，</span></span>可面上十分淡定<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯…<span><span>」</span></span> 我点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>冒昧请问<span><span>，</span></span>莫谷主的小叔叔叫什么名字<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫连风<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫英说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>鬼医莫连风<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我有些惊讶<span><span>。</span></span>然并非因为这个名字而惊讶<span><span>，</span></span>而是因为自己的糊涂而惊讶<span><span>。</span></span>昔日鬼医莫连风声名远播<span><span>，</span></span>有多少京都人氏往雪桑谷求医<span><span>。</span></span>姜叶颂的祖父就曾千里迢迢四顾雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>却连莫连风的面都没有见过<span><span>。</span></span>那莫连风死讯传出来的时候<span><span>，</span></span>有人惋惜有人嗤鼻<span><span>，</span></span>一时间议论纷纷<span><span>。</span></span>我怎么就把这号人物给忘了呢<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>此时<span><span>，</span></span>我懊悔中透着一丝兴奋<span><span>，</span></span>恨不得狠狠捏一把自己的大腿<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我正沉迷幻想无法自拔<span><span>，</span></span>那莫英却忽然问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>若你们抓住那只鬼<span><span>，</span></span>会怎么办<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>抓回地府…</p>
 <p>但我不能说<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>昆仑自有办法<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我只能胡乱应付道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫英蹙了蹙眉<span><span>，</span></span>低着头不知在想些什么<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>今夜我与师弟会在谷中布阵<span><span>。</span></span>为免鬼上人身<span><span>，</span></span>我会在所有房间前施法<span><span>，</span></span>烦请莫谷主知会所有人紧闭门窗<span><span>，</span></span>绝对不要出门<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫英爽快应下<span><span>。</span></span>随后又道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可否让我留在外面<span><span>。</span></span>我想见那鬼一面<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我决然拒绝<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>太危险了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可…<span><span>」</span></span> 莫英还要说话<span><span>，</span></span>却被我打断了<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>若要我昆仑帮忙<span><span>，</span></span>便按我说的做<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我和苏温在谷里上蹿下跳<span><span>，</span></span>拿出地府那套吓人的功夫<span><span>，</span></span>若叫他瞧了去<span><span>，</span></span>还不马上露馅儿<span><span>？</span></span>毕竟昆仑人家是名门正派<span><span>，</span></span>与地府的路数千差万别<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我可不想搬起石头砸自己的脚<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>又说了几句<span><span>，</span></span>我便拜别了莫英<span><span>。</span></span>我去了苏温房间<span><span>，</span></span>把发生的事跟他原原本本说了一遍<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>诅咒<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温皱了皱眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>听着比地府还邪门儿<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我的手指轻轻敲打着桌面<span><span>，</span></span>缓缓说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>这个倒不是我最奇怪的<span><span>。</span></span>让我最想不明白的是莫英为什么就认为那只鬼是他弟弟莫琼呢<span><span>？</span></span>我总觉得他还有什么事瞒着我<span><span>。</span></span>还有那个鬼…究竟是不是莫连风…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫连风…<span><span>」</span></span> 苏温点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>又摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>若真是莫连风…他为什么这么多年都不害人<span><span>，</span></span>突然就开始用这么残忍的方法害人了<span><span>？</span></span>难不成他在研究什么还阳术<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>还阳…<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我大吃一惊<span><span>，</span></span>即刻说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>烧张纸回去问问<span><span>，</span></span>异诡阁有没有鬼见过类似的记载<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>横空一捻<span><span>，</span></span>一张黄纸就被捏在了手中<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我又补充道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>对了<span><span>，</span></span>顺便问问<span><span>，</span></span>七年前莫琼是否已经被地府收走了<span><span>。</span></span>让他们尽快回复<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>地府异诡阁<span><span>，</span></span>养了一群懒鬼<span><span>。</span></span>虽说懒了些<span><span>，</span></span>可也是地府里最博学的一帮鬼<span><span>，</span></span>他们守着异诡阁的奇书异卷<span><span>，</span></span>通晓古今…有传闻<span><span>，</span></span>他们知道地府每一只鬼身后的秘密…</p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>7<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>夜色来临前<span><span>，</span></span>地府终于传回了消息<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>彼时<span><span>，</span></span>我正敷着俩黄瓜片儿在眼皮上<span><span>，</span></span>闭眼躺着<span><span>，</span></span>做战前准备<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>读读他们写什么了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我隔空挥了挥手<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>我听到苏温抖动黄纸的声音<span><span>。</span></span>又过了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>才听苏温说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>异诡阁说…活人血<span><span>，</span></span>可入药<span><span>。</span></span>而用活人的血当药引<span><span>，</span></span>古已有之<span><span>，</span></span>也不是什么新鲜事<span><span>，</span></span>本不值得小题大做<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>听罢<span><span>，</span></span>我额上三道黑线<span><span>。</span></span>看这笔触<span><span>，</span></span>必然是骆无极那老东西写的<span><span>。</span></span>凡作回答<span><span>，</span></span>必先踩你一句才算开始<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>往<span><span>，</span></span>往下念<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我手隔空比划着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦…<span><span>」</span></span> 伴随着又是一声纸抖的声音<span><span>，</span></span>苏温接着道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可若血尽而只剩干尸<span><span>，</span></span>则为诡术<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>苏温问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>诡术是什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>地府所有未命名的术法都被称为诡术<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我淡淡解惑道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这答案听着敷衍<span><span>，</span></span>可却实实在在<span><span>。</span></span>虽说说出口的那个瞬间<span><span>，</span></span>我也有那么一丝丝为地府感到羞愧与尴尬<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>咳咳…<span><span>」</span></span> 我挥一挥衣袖<span><span>，</span></span>从容道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>接着念<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>于是<span><span>，</span></span>苏温便又接着念道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>至阴之血<span><span>，</span></span>可引纯阳<span><span>，</span></span>此为记录在<span><span>《</span></span>十三凶煞•拂生引<span><span>》</span></span>中的一味药引<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span><span><span>《</span></span>十三凶煞•拂生引<span><span>》</span></span><span><span>？</span></span>那可真是有年头了…而且邪<span><span>，</span></span>太邪<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我惊呼<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我这一惊<span><span>，</span></span>差点惊落了两片水汪汪的黄瓜片儿<span><span>。</span></span>我正琢磨着<span><span>，</span></span>忽然听到苏温喃喃道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>随附死者生辰<span><span>，</span></span>暗语'多谢无极大人'…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>苏温一拳头锤在桌子上<span><span>。</span></span>闭眼睛都能感受到他有多无语<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>随后<span><span>，</span></span>听着一声儿极其不情愿的<span><span>「</span></span>多谢无极大人<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>嗖的一声儿<span><span>，</span></span>苏温接下了新来的黄纸<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人…<span><span>」</span></span> 苏温声音忽然严肃起来<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>从异诡阁送来的生辰看<span><span>，</span></span>那雪桑谷死的几个人<span><span>，</span></span>虽不同龄<span><span>，</span></span>却真的都是鬼月至阴时辰生人<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>至阴之血…<span><span>」</span></span> 我微微点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>他们有没有提到关于这药引<span><span>，</span></span>那<span><span>《</span></span>十三凶煞•拂生引<span><span>》</span></span>里都写了什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温念道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>说…三千年前<span><span>，</span></span>凡间曾盛行一种诡术<span><span>，</span></span>以至阴之血为引<span><span>，</span></span>辅以珍稀<span><span>，</span></span>施术炼制<span><span>，</span></span>能令病者愈<span><span>，</span></span>亡者生<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>珍稀<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我蹙了蹙眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>什么珍稀<span><span>？</span></span>是药材<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>异诡阁也不知道…但传闻是当时有个皇帝痴迷这种邪术<span><span>，</span></span>遍寻天下奇人异士为其炼制丹药<span><span>。</span></span>最后真的成功了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>成功了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我几乎要一跃而起<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>真是天下之大无奇不有<span><span>，</span></span>这鬼东西竟然都能让人给炼成<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我闭眼说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这么说来…那雪桑谷里<span><span>，</span></span>或人或鬼<span><span>，</span></span>是在练这诡术啊<span><span>！</span></span>病者愈也就罢了<span><span>，</span></span>亡者生…<span><span>？</span></span>这地府得是多憋屈啊…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温许久没有说话<span><span>，</span></span>屋子里忽然静悄悄的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>苏温<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我微微侧了侧头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>又过了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>在我几乎要忍不住摘下黄瓜片儿的时候<span><span>，</span></span>苏温忽然沉声儿道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>地府还回了信儿…关于莫琼<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>听苏温这鬼小子说话<span><span>，</span></span>真活活急死个鬼<span><span>。</span></span>我耐着性子<span><span>，</span></span>拖着长调问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫琼怎么了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我明显感觉到苏温吸了口气<span><span>，</span></span>幽幽道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫琼没有死<span><span>。</span></span>人历辛丑年腊月十八<span><span>，</span></span>地府带走的鬼<span><span>，</span></span>是莫英<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>8<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>彼时<span><span>，</span></span>我一把扔了黄瓜片儿<span><span>，</span></span>腾然坐起<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫英死了<span><span>？</span></span>那活着的…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>怪不得总觉得这莫英少了些少时的活泼<span><span>，</span></span>多了些稳重沉着<span><span>。</span></span>我还当是他成熟了许多<span><span>，</span></span>并未往其他方面去想过<span><span>。</span></span>还有<span><span>，</span></span>昔日莫英的天资明明不高<span><span>，</span></span>而如今却因医术超群而被称为医绝<span><span>。</span></span>原来在多年以前<span><span>，</span></span>莫英就不再是莫英<span><span>，</span></span>而是被莫琼替换了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人…<span><span>」</span></span> 苏温看我不说话<span><span>，</span></span>似乎有些发慌<span><span>，</span></span>压着嗓子问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你说…那莫琼究竟想干什么啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
