 <p><span><span>「</span></span>干什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我看向苏温<span><span>，</span></span>淡淡道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不管他要干什么<span><span>。</span></span>人<span><span>，</span></span>还能干过鬼么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可是…<span><span>」</span></span> 苏温挠了挠头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人…他们都说…有钱能使鬼推磨…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>闭嘴<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我瞪了苏温一眼<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>自揭老底<span><span>，</span></span>是鬼能干的事儿么<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温咧了咧嘴<span><span>，</span></span>而后又问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>要不要让地府查查当年究竟发生了什么事<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我蹙了蹙眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不<span><span>，</span></span>现在最重要的是莫连风<span><span>。</span></span>我们的任务<span><span>，</span></span>是把他带回地府<span><span>。</span></span>其他的<span><span>，</span></span>我们不应该管<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温深以为然<span><span>，</span></span>点了点头<span><span>。</span></span>可过了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>又偏过头问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>怎么说<span><span>，</span></span>当年你们也在一起待了那么长时间<span><span>。</span></span>你就不想知道当年发生了什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不想<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我简单明了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温似乎有些惊讶<span><span>，</span></span>轻轻晃了晃头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>你真绝<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我斜眼儿看向苏温<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我这怎么一时还听不出好赖话了呢…</p>
 <p>苏温没有理我<span><span>，</span></span>向外望了望<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>时辰差不多了<span><span>。</span></span>怎么还没有动静<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我侧耳听了听<span><span>，</span></span>的确是死样沉寂<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>该不会…大人…您那东西…不好用吧…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我冷笑了一声儿<span><span>，</span></span>一眼不眨地看着苏温<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你大人我死了三千一百四十三年零九个月又无数个时辰<span><span>。</span></span>能躲过苦陀铃的鬼<span><span>，</span></span>我至今还没见过<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温又听了听<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可是大人…真的不对劲儿啊<span><span>。</span></span>要不…出去看看<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我琢磨了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>终于点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>站起身来<span><span>，</span></span>摸了摸腰间的剑<span><span>，</span></span>挥了挥手<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>干活儿<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我和苏温并肩而行<span><span>，</span></span>身姿挺拔<span><span>、</span></span>步履生风<span><span>，</span></span>十分有气势地来到了死样沉寂的院子中<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>气势开得是够了<span><span>，</span></span>尴尬的事却发生了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人…是真没动静啊…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我闭上眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>仔细侧耳听着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>诶…别的院子也没有动静…</p>
 <p>我睁开眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>十分疑惑<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不可能…苦陀铃从未失过手<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温慢吞吞说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>其实大人你有没有想过…那鬼可能都没出现过<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看向苏温<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可那鬼没什么修为<span><span>，</span></span>白日里是出不来的<span><span>。</span></span>他白天不出来<span><span>，</span></span>晚上也不出来<span><span>。</span></span>他图什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>图…<span><span>」</span></span> 苏温支吾了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>也没谁出来个所以然<span><span>。</span></span>他说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>也许归玉城和昆仑惊动了他也说不定<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不可能<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我坚决否定他的推测<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>他连地府都不忌讳<span><span>，</span></span>还会忌讳归玉城和昆仑么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温还要说什么<span><span>，</span></span>却被我打断了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>行了<span><span>，</span></span>回去再说<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我低声儿说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我与苏温回了我的房间<span><span>。</span></span>我掩上了门<span><span>，</span></span>便道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>外面不安全<span><span>，</span></span>我不信任莫琼<span><span>，</span></span>也不知道那只老鬼是不是躲在暗处偷听<span><span>。</span></span>我们得小心点儿<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>谁能想到<span><span>，</span></span>我堂堂地府押魂使<span><span>，</span></span>竟沦落至此<span><span>。</span></span>抓只鬼回地府<span><span>，</span></span>都要偷偷摸摸<span><span>，</span></span>像做贼一样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我无奈问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>对了<span><span>，</span></span>你刚刚想说什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我是想问<span><span>，</span></span>那明日要如何同莫谷主说<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看了外面一眼<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>实话实说<span><span>，</span></span>便说鬼没有出现<span><span>。</span></span>想抓住那鬼<span><span>，</span></span>还需些时日<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温叹了口气<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>若非因为雪桑谷奇药众多<span><span>，</span></span>扰乱了咱们的嗅觉<span><span>。</span></span>想把他嗅出来<span><span>，</span></span>还不容易<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我眯了眯眼睛<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那莫连风恐怕就是抓住这点<span><span>，</span></span>才有恃无恐了这么多年<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那现在我们该怎么办<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我透过窗棂纸<span><span>，</span></span>穿过漆黑夜色<span><span>，</span></span>看着院中只有地府鬼差才能看见的苦陀铃<span><span>，</span></span>沉沉说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>还记得我说过么<span><span>，</span></span>他不离开雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>要么是走不了<span><span>，</span></span>要么是不愿意走<span><span>。</span></span>我今日瞧遍了雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>并没有什么厉害的阵法能将他困在这儿<span><span>。</span></span>那么便只能是第二种<span><span>，</span></span>他不愿意走<span><span>。</span></span>既是不愿意走<span><span>，</span></span>这谷中便有他留恋的东西<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温宛若醍醐灌顶<span><span>，</span></span>他点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>且这东西一定是他死了也带不走的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我蹙眉盯着苏温<span><span>，</span></span>有些嫌弃<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>当年你进三号牢房<span><span>，</span></span>没有鬼差训练过你么<span><span>？</span></span>人死了什么也带不走<span><span>。</span></span>你这不是说废话么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温不服气<span><span>，</span></span>继续推敲起来<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那…瞧着今天这架势<span><span>，</span></span>要么<span><span>，</span></span>这东西他已经找到了<span><span>。</span></span>要么这东西他不是在找<span><span>，</span></span>而是在等<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这话说得还真有点儿意思<span><span>。</span></span>我不自觉的弯起嘴角<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>管它是个什么东西<span><span>。</span></span>只要找到那个东西<span><span>，</span></span>拿在手中<span><span>。</span></span>我就不信<span><span>，</span></span>他莫连风不跟我们走<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温侧头看着我<span><span>，</span></span>半开玩笑问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那他要真的就不跟咱们走呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你恐怕想多了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我缓缓偏过头<span><span>，</span></span>回望向苏温<span><span>，</span></span>一字一字阴沉沉道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>这世上就没有我林拂收不了的鬼<span><span>、</span></span>办不结的差<span><span>。</span></span>莫连风若执意不跟我走<span><span>，</span></span>也没有旁的办法<span><span>。</span></span>先斩后奏<span><span>，</span></span>就让他在这雪桑谷中魂飞魄散<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我近乎变态般的眼神着实吓了苏温一跳<span><span>。</span></span>他摸了摸自己的脖颈<span><span>，</span></span>咳嗽了一声儿<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那个…大人…早歇着…我先回房了<span><span>。</span></span>明儿见…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>是一溜烟儿无影无踪<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>9<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>次日<span><span>，</span></span>我与苏温在正堂见到莫琼的时候<span><span>，</span></span>苏温这鬼小子那是相当露怯<span><span>。</span></span>他贼眉鼠眼悄悄打量人家莫琼<span><span>，</span></span>生怕别人看不出异样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我暗中捏了他后腰一把<span><span>，</span></span>低声儿道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>再整这没出息的出儿<span><span>，</span></span>回去扣你俸禄<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>果然<span><span>，</span></span>苏温一个激灵<span><span>，</span></span>又精神抖擞起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我转头看向莫琼<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫谷主<span><span>，</span></span>以昨日情形来看<span><span>，</span></span>想抓住那鬼<span><span>，</span></span>恐怕还需些时日<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>二位可见着那鬼了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温正想说话<span><span>，</span></span>我抢先答道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>见到了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温一愣<span><span>，</span></span>却也没有说话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼眼角微颤<span><span>，</span></span>有些急切问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可看清楚样子了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我故意又道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>与您确实很像…或者可以说是一模一样<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>我便紧盯着莫琼的脸<span><span>，</span></span>希望能看出什么<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>出乎意料的<span><span>，</span></span>他没有再提起那只鬼的身份<span><span>，</span></span>只是微微睁大眼睛问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>他都跟你们说什么了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我轻轻笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>莫谷主为什么这么问<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼此时回过神<span><span>，</span></span>似乎也发觉到自己的失态<span><span>。</span></span>于是端起一旁的茶盏<span><span>，</span></span>轻轻抿了一口<span><span>，</span></span>才说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>只是想听听吾弟阿琼<span><span>，</span></span>是否是还有什么心愿未了<span><span>，</span></span>才不肯离去<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>他说他的心愿与莫谷主有关<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我端起茶盏<span><span>，</span></span>故技重施<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>透过碗顶层层热气<span><span>，</span></span>我瞥见莫琼骤然苍白的脸色<span><span>，</span></span>以及闪烁了三下的眼睛<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一口茶喝进去<span><span>，</span></span>不等再有什么进展<span><span>，</span></span>忽听谷中弟子通传<span><span>，</span></span>说归玉城来了人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可知来了什么人<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫琼问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>前来通传的弟子脸成酱色<span><span>，</span></span>拱了拱手<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>归玉城城主<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>10<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>秦一迟跨进门来的时候<span><span>，</span></span>我差点认不出他<span><span>。</span></span>他比少时又瘦了许多<span><span>，</span></span>本就比常人要大的眼睛透出狠厉的光<span><span>，</span></span>后槽牙紧紧咬着<span><span>，</span></span>一进门就将手中的剑狠狠抛了出去<span><span>。</span></span>那剑径直飞了出去<span><span>，</span></span>擦过莫琼耳畔<span><span>，</span></span>死死扎在了他身后的墙壁之上<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>谷中弟子眼睛皆瞪<span><span>，</span></span>纷纷欲拔剑相向<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼伸出手<span><span>，</span></span>示意所有人不要动<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>秦兄…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼话刚说两个字<span><span>，</span></span>就被一阵冷喝怼了回去<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫英<span><span>！</span></span>这就是答应的安然无恙<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着功夫<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟又一把拔下那扎在墙上的剑<span><span>，</span></span>死死抵在莫琼的脖颈处<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼微微抬眼<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>秦兄<span><span>，</span></span>是我雪桑谷连累了令弟<span><span>。</span></span>如果你要取我性命<span><span>，</span></span>我也无话可说<span><span>。</span></span>只是如今最重要的平息祸事<span><span>，</span></span>还雪桑谷安宁<span><span>，</span></span>也让令弟亡魂得以安息<span><span>。</span></span>等一切平定<span><span>，</span></span>我莫英甘受你这一剑<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟的眼里燃烧着一团怒火<span><span>，</span></span>持剑的手微微抖动着<span><span>，</span></span>就那么死死盯着莫琼的眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>咬着牙冷冷道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>莫英<span><span>，</span></span>这事情没完<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟终于收回了剑<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我弟弟在哪儿<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>已经安顿好了<span><span>。</span></span>秦兄可以随我去看<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟走前<span><span>，</span></span>眼锋一扫<span><span>，</span></span>扫见我时微微一愣<span><span>，</span></span>可他没说话<span><span>，</span></span>只是狐疑地看了我一眼<span><span>，</span></span>便疾步离开了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>灵堂空旷<span><span>，</span></span>棺木散发着地府的凄冷感<span><span>，</span></span>就连那几个守棺人的气息都显得阴沉沉的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一行死得实在太惨了<span><span>，</span></span>我如此铁石心肠的一只鬼在一旁瞧着都心里一阵异样<span><span>，</span></span>更不要说秦一迟<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那秦一迟脸色发青<span><span>，</span></span>提剑的那一整只手臂都在以肉眼可见的程度颤抖着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么时候才能抓住那只鬼<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟自打踏进雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>一口牙就没松开过<span><span>。</span></span>他紧紧盯着莫琼<span><span>，</span></span>明显是要一个许诺<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这鬼连归玉城都对付不了<span><span>，</span></span>现…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼话没说完<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟便冷冷打断了他<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你说这意思<span><span>，</span></span>倒是我归玉城的不是了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼蹙了蹙眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>话还是没说完<span><span>，</span></span>便又被秦一迟狠心打断<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>雪桑谷打算如何给我交代<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>介绍道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这二位是昆仑的高徒<span><span>。</span></span>昨日已经会过…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>昆仑…<span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟看向我<span><span>，</span></span>再一次打断了莫琼的话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我有理由相信<span><span>，</span></span>这小子是故意的<span><span>。</span></span>因为他小时候就这样<span><span>，</span></span>一丝一毫都吃不得亏<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>昆仑林拂<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我拱了拱手<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>苏温<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温也拱了拱手<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟微微点头<span><span>，</span></span>只看了一眼苏温<span><span>，</span></span>目光便又停留在我的身上<span><span>。</span></span>他说<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>林姑娘<span><span>，</span></span>不知莫谷主有没有说过<span><span>，</span></span>你长得很像我们的一个故人<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我毫不闪躲地看着秦一迟<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>的确说过<span><span>。</span></span>如今连秦城主都这样说<span><span>，</span></span>看来是真的很像<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟没再说什么<span><span>，</span></span>只又看了那惨死鬼的尸身一眼<span><span>，</span></span>便对我道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我弟弟死之前的事<span><span>，</span></span>我大概知道一二<span><span>。</span></span>后面的事<span><span>，</span></span>还要劳烦姑娘告知在下<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 而后<span><span>，</span></span>又微微侧头<span><span>，</span></span>阴阳怪气道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还望莫谷主也要知无不言<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>竟带着头提剑离开了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>回到正堂<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟的脸依然臭得要命<span><span>。</span></span>屋内许久没人说话<span><span>，</span></span>苏温似乎如坐针毡<span><span>，</span></span>屁股一直翘起来又落下<span><span>，</span></span>落下去又扭起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我咳嗽了一声儿<span><span>，</span></span>看向苏温<span><span>。</span></span>他立马消停了<span><span>，</span></span>估计是想到了自己可怜的俸禄<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我这一声咳嗽打破沉寂<span><span>。</span></span>不大一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟便开口问了我关于闹鬼的事<span><span>。</span></span>我藏着掖着说了一堆<span><span>，</span></span>而后又看向莫琼<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫谷主<span><span>，</span></span>关于雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>我还有几个问题要请教<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>但问无妨<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>第一个问题<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我肃色端坐<span><span>，</span></span>沉声问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>莫谷主听说过以人血为引的古方么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼微微愣了一下<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>听是听过<span><span>，</span></span>只是正统医书上从未有过明确的记载<span><span>。</span></span>偏症杂书倒是有<span><span>，</span></span>可也只是寥寥<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>话音落下<span><span>，</span></span>莫琼接着便问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怎么<span><span>？</span></span>这与那鬼害人的事有关么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这个莫琼<span><span>，</span></span>怎么就打定好了<span><span>，</span></span>一定就是那鬼在害人<span><span>？</span></span>不能是…人害人么<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>想着<span><span>，</span></span>我说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没什么<span><span>，</span></span>各种可能性都要考虑的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 说完<span><span>，</span></span>我又问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>第二个问题<span><span>，</span></span>当年的鬼医莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>也就是您的叔叔<span><span>，</span></span>是怎么死的<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>记得之前我提到过<span><span>，</span></span>莫家子孙是受到诅咒的<span><span>。</span></span>我叔叔也是恶疾缠身<span><span>，</span></span>不治而亡<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫连风可有什么非常珍贵的东西<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼微微蹙眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>珍贵…的东西<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我点头道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>对<span><span>，</span></span>珍贵的东西<span><span>。</span></span>珍贵到可能连死都要带进坟墓<span><span>，</span></span>带下地府的东西<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼想了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>缓缓摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我小叔叔为人清冷孤僻<span><span>，</span></span>没有妻儿<span><span>，</span></span>没什么朋友<span><span>，</span></span>也没什么喜好<span><span>。</span></span>好像所有凡尘俗物于他而言都只是过眼云烟<span><span>，</span></span>即便是他最擅长的医术…他也并不在意…死前半月<span><span>，</span></span>还一把火烧光了毕生所写的所有医书<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>为什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我一愣<span><span>，</span></span>随后说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我的意思是…即便他再淡泊名利<span><span>，</span></span>也没必要把所有医书烧了啊<span><span>。</span></span>留给雪桑谷难道不好么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼苦笑着摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没人能真正看透我这个小叔叔<span><span>。</span></span>连家父都不能<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼说完<span><span>，</span></span>忽然回过神来<span><span>，</span></span>问我道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>林姑娘为何突然问起我小叔叔<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>，</span></span>没什么<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>鬼医莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>昔日谁人不知谁人不晓<span><span>。</span></span>我只是单纯得好奇罢了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>还不等莫琼开口说什么<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟便截了胡<span><span>。</span></span>他好像很惊讶<span><span>，</span></span>但我认识他许多年了<span><span>，</span></span>一眼就看出那表情是装出来的<span><span>。</span></span>他装作好奇<span><span>，</span></span>实际上是一肚子坏水儿<span><span>，</span></span>此时幽幽问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>是么<span><span>？</span></span>可瞧着林姑娘年纪不大<span><span>，</span></span>鬼医莫连风盛名在外之时<span><span>，</span></span>你应该还没出生<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>虽不知道他这番阴阳怪气要干什么<span><span>。</span></span>但他有他的张良计<span><span>，</span></span>我有我的过墙梯<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着秦一迟<span><span>，</span></span>十分从容回道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>自幼便听昆仑的前辈讲起过鬼医的故事<span><span>。</span></span>他这样的人<span><span>，</span></span>生前荣耀<span><span>，</span></span>死而盛名不减<span><span>。</span></span>不是么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟没再说什么<span><span>，</span></span>可他看了我许久<span><span>，</span></span>久到我已经如坐针毡<span><span>，</span></span>恨不得拿条布蒙住他的眼睛<span><span>。</span></span>又过了好一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>他才收回目光<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>三日<span><span>，</span></span>只有三日<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟看向莫英<span><span>，</span></span>凛声道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你雪桑谷的事我管不着<span><span>，</span></span>也不想管<span><span>。</span></span>但我弟弟的死<span><span>，</span></span>我要一个交代<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>不等回复<span><span>，</span></span>便起身提剑而去<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>11<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>秦一迟走后<span><span>，</span></span>莫琼的脸色也不大好看<span><span>。</span></span>过了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>他忽然问我道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那个鬼<span><span>，</span></span>真的是我弟弟么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我含糊回道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>都是猜测<span><span>，</span></span>他说的不清不楚<span><span>。</span></span>但言语之间<span><span>，</span></span>我觉得…事情应该和你小叔叔还有些关系<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span><span>，</span></span>我看向莫琼<span><span>，</span></span>希望能再从他口中套出些话来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>怪不得你问了我小叔叔的事<span><span>。</span></span>原来<span><span>，</span></span>也并非是随口问问<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫琼说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我唇角咧了一下<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>对鬼医的好奇的确是真的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>好奇当然是真的<span><span>。</span></span>因为那鬼就是莫连风啊<span><span>！</span></span>我能不好奇么<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>好奇之下<span><span>，</span></span>我又引导道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>莫谷主不妨再仔细回忆一下<span><span>，</span></span>您叔叔莫连风就真的没什么特别珍贵的<span><span>，</span></span>或者…死后没留下什么东西么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>以我三千多年天上地下摸爬滚打的锐利眼光看去<span><span>，</span></span>莫琼神色有那么片刻的异常<span><span>。</span></span>虽稍纵即逝<span><span>，</span></span>但的确是有<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼一定在隐藏什么<span><span>。</span></span>不仅关于莫英<span><span>，</span></span>也关于莫连风<span><span>。</span></span>可他这小子<span><span>，</span></span>藏得极深<span><span>。</span></span>若是鬼我有的是办法让他开口<span><span>。</span></span>可他是个大活人<span><span>，</span></span>地府那套<span><span>，</span></span>对付不了他<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那抹异样神色转瞬消逝后<span><span>，</span></span>莫琼露出惋惜神色<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我已经说了<span><span>，</span></span>我小叔叔这个人<span><span>。</span></span>没人看得透他<span><span>。</span></span>他也不信任任何人<span><span>。</span></span>所以<span><span>，</span></span>他的事<span><span>，</span></span>我真的不知道<span><span>。</span></span>唯一可能留下来的医书<span><span>，</span></span>也尽数毁于火海<span><span>。</span></span>除了一世盛名<span><span>，</span></span>我这小叔叔恐怕什么也没有留下<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他都如此说了<span><span>，</span></span>看来再问也问不出什么了<span><span>。</span></span>于是我对苏温使了个眼色<span><span>，</span></span>打算打道回府<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>与莫琼分别<span><span>，</span></span>我与苏温又钻回了房间<span><span>。</span></span>屁股刚一落在凳子上<span><span>，</span></span>苏温便问<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>你觉得莫连风晚上会出现么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>很难说<span><span>。</span></span>所以我们要尽快找出他留恋的东西<span><span>，</span></span>才能捏住他命门<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温叹了口气<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可我们现在连那东西的影儿都没摸到<span><span>。</span></span>此前我还想着<span><span>，</span></span>他许是个医痴<span><span>，</span></span>死了还在继续研究医术<span><span>，</span></span>甚至…是诡术<span><span>。</span></span>可他既然死前一把火烧了医书<span><span>，</span></span>便可见牵绊他的不是这些东西<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>喉咙一滚<span><span>，</span></span>感觉嗓子眼儿里像噎了什么东西<span><span>。</span></span>恐怕是上了火<span><span>，</span></span>给愁的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我捏着嗓子说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可惜那莫连风生平太过孤僻<span><span>，</span></span>与他有交往的人寥寥无几不说<span><span>，</span></span>还都是泛泛往来<span><span>。</span></span>唯一在世的亲人<span><span>，</span></span>还说自己也看不透他<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>听听…莫连风他还是个人么<span><span>？</span></span>活着就像只鬼的<span><span>，</span></span>他是我见的头一个<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人啊…你说…这事儿什么时候才能结啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温拄着下巴<span><span>，</span></span>幽然叹息<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温如此愁眉不展<span><span>，</span></span>我作为他的老大<span><span>，</span></span>必须给他吃颗定心丸<span><span>。</span></span>于是我非常认真得看向苏温<span><span>，</span></span>稳稳说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你放心<span><span>。</span></span>有我在<span><span>，</span></span>绝不让你在这劳什子地方多待<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>此时苏温眼底一亮<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>下一秒<span><span>，</span></span>我严肃道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>再等三日<span><span>，</span></span>还没头绪<span><span>，</span></span>便直接让他魂飞魄散<span><span>。</span></span> <span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温张开嘴巴又闭上<span><span>，</span></span>闭上又张开<span><span>。</span></span>如此两个会和<span><span>，</span></span>终于蹙眉说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我说大人<span><span>！</span></span>你怎么就动不动魂飞魄散的<span><span>？</span></span>文明点儿<span><span>，</span></span>平和点儿<span><span>，</span></span>友爱点儿<span><span>，</span></span>行不行<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我不文明<span><span>？</span></span>我不平和<span><span>？</span></span>我不友爱<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我瞪着眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>一拳头锤在桌子上<span><span>，</span></span>震得满桌茶碗跳了脚<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>我知道<span><span>，</span></span>阎王大人是您义兄<span><span>，</span></span>您倒是不怕<span><span>。</span></span>但是我们三号牢房的兄弟们怕啊<span><span>！</span></span>到最后功德没积成就算了<span><span>，</span></span>可别再折损些<span><span>。</span></span>若是那样<span><span>，</span></span>兄弟几个可没地方哭去<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这话说得…我也要积功德的<span><span>。</span></span>怎么听着<span><span>，</span></span>就像我是个整日欺行霸市的地府关系户<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那你不是说…你想回地府吗<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我说话有些结巴<span><span>，</span></span>可却气势汹汹得盯着苏温<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温一脸无语<span><span>，</span></span>淡淡说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我何时说了想回地府<span><span>？</span></span>我是问大人觉得何时才能了结此事<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我哑巴吃黄连<span><span>，</span></span>只能瞪眼捶胸<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温这边又张开嘴<span><span>，</span></span>可话还没说出口<span><span>。</span></span>忽然<span><span>，</span></span>门边响起了极其细微却清晰的敲门声<span><span>。</span></span>与其说是敲门声<span><span>，</span></span>不如说是敲打木框的声音<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我伸手制止了要发出声音的苏温<span><span>。</span></span>侧耳细细听去<span><span>，</span></span>那一声一声缓慢而有节奏<span><span>，</span></span>每一下都敲打在我的心脏上<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我感觉自己心梗了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>因为我听出了节奏下的<span><span>，</span></span>那阔别多年的暗语<span><span>，</span></span>说的正是<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姜叶颂<span><span>，</span></span>酉时三刻<span><span>，</span></span>假山相见<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>12<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>我没有去假山<span><span>。</span></span>去了就是不打自招<span><span>，</span></span>谁去谁是傻子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>当夜<span><span>，</span></span>鬼还是没有出现<span><span>，</span></span>但不妨碍我一整晚没有睡<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>人间即便到了夜晚<span><span>，</span></span>也比地府阳气重得多得多<span><span>。</span></span>可雪桑谷不一样<span><span>，</span></span>这里药气重<span><span>，</span></span>阴气更重<span><span>。</span></span>所以当年做姜叶颂的时候<span><span>，</span></span>我非常喜欢这里<span><span>，</span></span>因为这里总让我想起地府<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那时候莫英身子骨不好<span><span>，</span></span>活是一副病秧子模样<span><span>。</span></span>秦一迟便总半开玩笑说让他离开雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>多去<span><span>「</span></span>人间<span><span>」</span></span>走走<span><span>。</span></span>说起那个暗语<span><span>，</span></span>还是秦一迟发明的<span><span>。</span></span>昔日几个人不过十五六岁的年纪<span><span>，</span></span>总喜欢窃窃说些悄悄话<span><span>，</span></span>不愿别人听了去<span><span>，</span></span>于是便常以这种方式约定见面的时间和地点<span><span>。</span></span>那时候我觉得他相当幼稚<span><span>，</span></span>可糊里糊涂得也跟他们用暗语比划了好些年<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>如今再听见<span><span>，</span></span>当真有种恍若隔世的感觉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>想着这些<span><span>，</span></span>我睁着眼睛干巴巴等到了天亮<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>第二天<span><span>，</span></span>我刚一跨进正堂<span><span>，</span></span>那秦一迟便抬头瞧了我一眼<span><span>。</span></span>其实就一眼<span><span>，</span></span>但我似乎是做贼心虚<span><span>，</span></span>心脏狂跳不止<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可我这鬼<span><span>，</span></span>心里越是慌乱<span><span>，</span></span>脸上反倒越是平静<span><span>，</span></span>甚至可能还有些不可言说的臭脸子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>坐下后<span><span>，</span></span>我便问莫琼道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>昨日给莫谷主的那些汤药<span><span>，</span></span>可叫谷中诸位饮下了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我与秦兄已经喝下<span><span>，</span></span>并分给所有谷中弟子了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 而后又问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>冒昧问一句<span><span>，</span></span>姑娘说那汤药能防鬼上身<span><span>。</span></span>究竟是些什么药方<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>自不是普通药方<span><span>，</span></span>是珍稀药引加以昆仑的秘术<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我点到而止<span><span>，</span></span>非常淡定地看着莫琼<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>其实也没什么特别<span><span>，</span></span>那汤药实则是黄泉一抔土<span><span>，</span></span>咸燥苦涩<span><span>，</span></span>可能顺便还带了些人骨头味儿<span><span>。</span></span>刚死的鬼最怕这味道<span><span>，</span></span>黄泉的味道<span><span>。</span></span>听说<span><span>，</span></span>在幽冥族的古语里<span><span>，</span></span>这种味道有一个独特的名字<span><span>，</span></span>叫作<span><span>「</span></span>阿陀麼<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>意为<span><span>：</span></span>不确定的未来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这黄泉土汤当然可以让鬼不敢上人身<span><span>。</span></span>可我想要的却不止于此<span><span>。</span></span>他莫连风既想躲<span><span>，</span></span>那就躲好了<span><span>。</span></span>可我要让这雪桑谷中沾满<span><span>「</span></span>阿陀麼<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>我要让他知道<span><span>，</span></span>抓他的人已经来了<span><span>，</span></span>且不是个善茬儿<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>既不能悄无声息得给他带走<span><span>，</span></span>那就看谁玩儿得过谁<span><span>。</span></span>我堂堂地府第一押魂使<span><span>，</span></span>对付不了一个死了十几年的鬼<span><span>，</span></span>说出去<span><span>，</span></span>我不要面子的<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>想着<span><span>，</span></span>我露出坏笑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>当我正沉浸对自己的敬佩中<span><span>。</span></span>那秦一迟非常不客气得开了口<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫谷主<span><span>，</span></span>昨日那半天我姑且不算<span><span>。</span></span>自今日起<span><span>，</span></span>三日你可要算好了<span><span>。</span></span>三日后若还没有交代<span><span>，</span></span>我不确定我会做出什么<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟这小子<span><span>，</span></span>又开始装象<span><span>。</span></span>他们归玉城的术法虽说不如昆仑<span><span>，</span></span>可也不至于干等着别人抓鬼<span><span>。</span></span>他真是逮着机会就要恫吓莫琼几句<span><span>，</span></span>似乎这样<span><span>，</span></span>他就为他弟弟报仇了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫琼叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>口中信誓旦旦<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>秦兄放心<span><span>，</span></span>我一定还令弟一个公道<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>很好<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟满意得点了下头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我心里无限惆怅<span><span>，</span></span>更觉得好笑<span><span>。</span></span>这俩人纯属于嘴行千里<span><span>，</span></span>屁股在家<span><span>。</span></span>就他俩天天早上会晤一下<span><span>，</span></span>一个放放狠话<span><span>，</span></span>一个满口保证<span><span>，</span></span>就这<span><span>？</span></span>这就抓着鬼了<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>无语<span><span>！</span></span>狂妄<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我暗自翻了个白眼儿<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那一边<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟得到了满意的答案<span><span>，</span></span>浑身放松起来<span><span>。</span></span>只见他细长的手指慢慢敲打起了桌面<span><span>，</span></span>一声接着一声儿<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那细长手指敲打出的暗语说的是<span><span>：</span></span>半炷香后<span><span>，</span></span>羡云亭来聚<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我咬着牙<span><span>，</span></span>装作什么也没听见<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>敲完不久<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟缓缓起身<span><span>，</span></span>状若无意得开口道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>想来<span><span>，</span></span>我小师父的冥诞也快到了<span><span>。</span></span>今年也许赶得及在此祭拜<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我狐疑得看了秦一迟一眼<span><span>，</span></span>却什么也没问<span><span>。</span></span>莫琼在一旁似乎是瞧见了<span><span>，</span></span>便解释道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>对了<span><span>，</span></span>林姑娘可能不知道<span><span>，</span></span>秦城主很小的时候曾跟我小叔叔学过几个月的医术<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>一日为师终身为师<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟深深看了我一眼<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你说呢<span><span>？</span></span>林姑娘<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这个秦一迟<span><span>，</span></span>知道我想打听莫连风的事<span><span>，</span></span>如今明显是在暗示我他知道一些事<span><span>，</span></span>甚至可能比莫琼还要清楚<span><span>。</span></span>可我此前从未听他提起过此事<span><span>，</span></span>还有…我问莫琼关于莫连风的事<span><span>，</span></span>也从未听他说过秦一迟竟是莫连风的徒弟<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我正想着<span><span>，</span></span>忽听秦一迟喊我名字<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>林姑娘<span><span>，</span></span>莫谷主<span><span>。</span></span>回见<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这<span><span>「</span></span>回见<span><span>」</span></span>二字意味深长<span><span>，</span></span>我看着秦一迟离开的背影<span><span>，</span></span>如鲠在喉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他走后<span><span>，</span></span>我心乱如麻<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>此刻苏温正对雪桑谷进行地毯式搜索<span><span>。</span></span>若他能搜出些什么…当然了<span><span>，</span></span>八成是搜不到的<span><span>。</span></span>所以我们手里关于莫连风的线索实在太少了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我也想过秦一迟可能在使诈<span><span>。</span></span>毕竟他小时候就已经有些狡诈的苗头了<span><span>，</span></span>这些年恐怕已经可以用<span><span>「</span></span>老奸巨猾<span><span>」</span></span>来形容了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可我一只鬼<span><span>，</span></span>一只束手无策的鬼<span><span>。</span></span>我光脚不怕穿鞋的啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>想着想着<span><span>，</span></span>我鬼心一横<span><span>。</span></span>管他是骗人还是真心<span><span>。</span></span>姑且见他一面<span><span>。</span></span>我一只摸爬滚打三千多年的鬼<span><span>，</span></span>还怕他区区一个脆弱的人类么<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>13<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>这边跟莫琼分别<span><span>，</span></span>我便急匆匆往羡云亭去了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>羡云亭是雪桑谷中位置最为偏僻的亭子<span><span>。</span></span>它位于一处山体夹缝<span><span>，</span></span>平日里很少有人会出现在那里<span><span>。</span></span>多年以前<span><span>，</span></span>他们几个总是躲在这儿偷偷喝酒<span><span>，</span></span>喝得半醉不醉<span><span>，</span></span>开始舞刀弄剑<span><span>、</span></span>吟诗作对<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那时候我就总在想<span><span>，</span></span>人啊<span><span>，</span></span>不仅肉体脆弱<span><span>，</span></span>灵魂还多愁善感…没救了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>想着想着<span><span>，</span></span>抄近路走了不到半炷香的功夫<span><span>，</span></span>便到了羡云亭外<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>好家伙<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟竟然还没来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>以前每每相聚于此<span><span>，</span></span>就数他动作最慢<span><span>。</span></span>如今凡间过了多少年<span><span>，</span></span>他还是这样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>缓步踏上了石阶<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可我这脚刚踏上去就后悔了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>仔细想想<span><span>，</span></span>莫连风的事同他弟弟的死可能有关<span><span>。</span></span>若他知道什么<span><span>，</span></span>我就不信他到时候不说<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>到底是我太心急<span><span>，</span></span>自露出马脚来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>现在撤<span><span>，</span></span>也不知道是否来得及…</p>
 <p>我还来不及动作<span><span>，</span></span>忽闻男声<span><span>，</span></span>淡淡轻笑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>装够了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我没回头<span><span>，</span></span>双腿开始发沉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姜叶颂<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他忽然叫道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我不想理他<span><span>，</span></span>可我的脚不由自主地顿住了<span><span>，</span></span>极其没有出息<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>脚步声越来越近<span><span>，</span></span>那人自我身后绕到了我面前<span><span>。</span></span>竟是秦一迟眸中带光<span><span>，</span></span>嘴角含笑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>秦城主在叫我<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我开始装傻<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>都说了别装了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟似乎很瞧不上我的伎俩似的<span><span>，</span></span>哼道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>若非听见暗语<span><span>，</span></span>你怎么会出现在这儿<span><span>？</span></span>别跟我说<span><span>，</span></span>你是随便逛过来的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我没说话<span><span>，</span></span>他便接着又道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你那些说辞骗骗别人也就罢了<span><span>。</span></span>我是绝对不会相信世上会有两个长得完全一样的人的<span><span>。</span></span>更何况<span><span>，</span></span>你的举止仪态<span><span>，</span></span>与姜叶颂那是一模一样<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我无语<span><span>，</span></span>非常无语<span><span>，</span></span>极其无语<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这玩意是真的太聪明<span><span>，</span></span>还是瞎猫碰上了死耗子<span><span>，</span></span>怎么就让他给我逮了个现行儿呢<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>现在拔腿跑吧<span><span>，</span></span>绝对坐实了心虚<span><span>。</span></span>矢口否认吧<span><span>，</span></span>我又太了解秦一迟的个性<span><span>，</span></span>他若咬死了什么事儿或者什么人<span><span>，</span></span>达不到他满意的效果是绝对不会撒口的<span><span>。</span></span>到时候惊动了莫琼还好说<span><span>，</span></span>要是闹得那老鬼彻底躲起来<span><span>，</span></span>我这差事算是交不上了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>于是<span><span>，</span></span>我决定早死早托生<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我抬起头<span><span>，</span></span>淡淡笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>秦一迟<span><span>，</span></span>好久不见<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟看着我<span><span>，</span></span>挑了挑眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>倒也不是很久<span><span>，</span></span>只是九年零七个月而已<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我没有说话<span><span>，</span></span>也不知道应该说什么<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟轻淡问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>说说吧<span><span>，</span></span>你是什么情况<span><span>？</span></span>昆仑又是怎么回事<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我刚说一个字<span><span>，</span></span>就被秦一迟夺过话头<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你该不会是鬼吧<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span><span>，</span></span>要来掐我的脸<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我隔空打掉秦一迟的手<span><span>，</span></span>警告道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你再动手动脚<span><span>，</span></span>我砍了你的胳膊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哈…<span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟满意得点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不愧是姜叶颂<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 说罢<span><span>，</span></span>又问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>看你这些年也没什么变化<span><span>？</span></span>总归不是假死<span><span>。</span></span>到底怎么回事儿<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我皮笑肉不笑<span><span>，</span></span>佯作坦然道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>七年前我是死了<span><span>。</span></span> 可我死后拜入昆仑<span><span>，</span></span>诚心修行<span><span>，</span></span>如今只盼一日飞升<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>飞升<span><span>？</span></span>昆仑<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟笑了一下<span><span>，</span></span>又仔细打量我几眼<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可我怎么瞧你<span><span>，</span></span>都是鬼里鬼气的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我这心是拔拔凉啊…秦一迟这小子难不成是鬼王给我设的拦路障<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>心里没底<span><span>，</span></span>可脸上从容<span><span>。</span></span>我镇静得抖了抖衣袖<span><span>，</span></span>盯着秦一迟道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>九年不见<span><span>，</span></span>你是不盼我一点好<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟淡淡一笑<span><span>，</span></span>缓步向身后的石坐走去<span><span>，</span></span>边走边说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>当年李穆禾因你而死<span><span>，</span></span>我恨过你来着<span><span>。</span></span>不过我也知道<span><span>，</span></span>不是你的错<span><span>，</span></span>是闵荀<span><span>。</span></span>所以听说你死了<span><span>，</span></span>我还是很难过的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>话音刚落<span><span>，</span></span>没给我说话的机会<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟便又道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>如今看来<span><span>，</span></span>倒是可惜了我的眼泪<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我觉得这一次我已经张嘴很快了<span><span>，</span></span>却还是被他无情打断<span><span>。</span></span>他的手指轻轻敲打着椅子边儿<span><span>，</span></span>缓缓说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你说…我弟弟…还有李穆禾他们…也会像你这样<span><span>，</span></span>再回来么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着他的眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>心底的一股火骤然就被熄灭了<span><span>，</span></span>一时间甚至不知该说些什么<span><span>。</span></span>过了许久<span><span>，</span></span>我沉缓说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>鬼祖檀骊曾经说过<span><span>，</span></span>来不及道别的终将再次重逢<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟眼底骤然涌上一层薄雾<span><span>。</span></span>他缓缓点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>嘴角露出一抹笑意<span><span>。</span></span>可只笑了片刻<span><span>，</span></span>他忽然盯着我道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>谁<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你说谁说<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟蹙了蹙眉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊…<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我装傻充愣<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>言多必失<span><span>，</span></span>我真是大意了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟不肯作罢<span><span>，</span></span>他问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你是说…鬼祖<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我振振道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你听错了<span><span>，</span></span>我说的是老祖<span><span>，</span></span>昆仑老祖<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟还要说什么<span><span>，</span></span>被我给打断了<span><span>。</span></span>我不耐烦道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>行了<span><span>，</span></span>说正事<span><span>。</span></span>你知道莫连风的事<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟没再纠缠鬼祖的事<span><span>，</span></span>可也没直接回答我<span><span>，</span></span>而是看着我道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我先问你一个问题<span><span>。</span></span>那只鬼真的是莫琼么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我没有说话<span><span>，</span></span>我在想应该怎么骗他<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可他却道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那鬼是莫英对不对<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我愣住了<span><span>，</span></span>还是没说话<span><span>。</span></span>这次<span><span>，</span></span>我是语塞<span><span>，</span></span>不知道该说些什么<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟见我不回应<span><span>，</span></span>轻轻摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你不要骗我<span><span>。</span></span>其实早很多年<span><span>，</span></span>我就猜到真正的莫英可能已经死了<span><span>。</span></span>他是什么样的人我最清楚<span><span>。</span></span>医术上<span><span>，</span></span>他没什么天份<span><span>，</span></span>也并不想继承家学<span><span>。</span></span>可他重情重义<span><span>，</span></span>李穆禾死的时候<span><span>，</span></span>身上背着多少污名<span><span>，</span></span>他都跋山涉水相送<span><span>，</span></span>毫无畏惧<span><span>。</span></span>可是你死的时候<span><span>，</span></span>他没有来<span><span>。</span></span>今日…他也没有来<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说到这里<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟喉咙一哽<span><span>，</span></span>看着我的眼睛微微透着红<span><span>，</span></span>声音都有些嘶哑了<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>现在的莫英是他弟弟莫琼<span><span>，</span></span>对不对<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>现在这时候再瞒下去也没什么必要<span><span>。</span></span>于是我只说了一个字<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>是<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟脸色苍白<span><span>，</span></span>极其缓慢得点了点头<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫琼死信传来的时候<span><span>，</span></span>我就觉得奇怪<span><span>。</span></span>我赶了两天两夜来到这里<span><span>，</span></span>想看看有什么可以帮忙<span><span>。</span></span>可是那个时候莫琼的尸身就已经下葬了<span><span>。</span></span>不足七日<span><span>，</span></span>如此匆忙<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我心里一怔<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你是说…莫琼…或者说是莫英死的时候不足七日就匆忙下葬<span><span>，</span></span>可知道原因<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟叹息道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>说是莫琼的遗愿<span><span>，</span></span>不愿尸体发臭…可我总觉得十分勉强<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>既觉得勉强又古怪<span><span>，</span></span>为何没弄清楚<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟苦笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>因为我不敢多想…姜叶颂…我不知你在昆仑待了多久…也不知你是否真的待在昆仑<span><span>。</span></span>但你可知道…人间的十年有多么漫长<span><span>？</span></span>你和李穆禾都死了<span><span>，</span></span>闵荀也疯了…如果莫英也死了<span><span>，</span></span>那这世上也再没什么意思了<span><span>。</span></span>所以在那之后我便不再和他联系<span><span>。</span></span>好像只有这样<span><span>，</span></span>我便可以永远不必正视这件事<span><span>。</span></span>直到几个月前雪桑谷来信<span><span>，</span></span>请我弟弟帮他们驱除鬼魅邪祟…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>听到这儿<span><span>，</span></span>我忽然精神起来<span><span>，</span></span>蹙眉问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你说…是莫琼要你弟弟来的<span><span>？</span></span>他是指了名的要秦一行来雪桑谷么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>因为梵音铃只有我们秦家人会用<span><span>。</span></span>而我是城主<span><span>，</span></span>不便前往<span><span>。</span></span>所以他便找上了阿行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>若他是故意的呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我幽幽说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟不解地看着我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我没回答他<span><span>，</span></span>而是又问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你可还记得当年第一个发现莫琼…或者说莫英尸体的人<span><span>，</span></span>是谁<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟想了想<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是莫英<span><span>。</span></span>不…莫琼<span><span>。</span></span>而且彼时莫连声莫谷主已经病得非常重了<span><span>。</span></span>一切都是莫琼主持大局<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟刚说完<span><span>，</span></span>还不等我开口<span><span>，</span></span>他便突兀问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你也怀疑…是莫琼害死了莫英<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>也<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我看向秦一迟<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟叹道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>昔日老谷主中意的一直都是莫英<span><span>。</span></span>即便他天资不高<span><span>，</span></span>也不妨碍他成为未来的谷主<span><span>。</span></span>老谷主的偏爱谁人不知<span><span>？</span></span>若莫英还活着<span><span>，</span></span>哪里能轮的上他弟弟莫琼<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我摇了摇头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>虽说我与莫琼当年算不得要好<span><span>。</span></span>但我总觉得单单是一个谷主的位子<span><span>，</span></span>倒不至于让他对自己的兄长痛下杀手<span><span>。</span></span>所以我还有一件事要确认<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫英的生辰…你还记得么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>他同阿行同月同日同时辰<span><span>，</span></span>我当然记得<span><span>。</span></span>何况当年…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟话说一半<span><span>，</span></span>忽然瞪眼看着我<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不对啊…姜叶颂<span><span>，</span></span>你死了就算了<span><span>，</span></span>你连莫英的生日都忘了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我没理他<span><span>，</span></span>任由他在一旁吹胡子瞪眼<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>与秦一行同月同日同时辰<span><span>，</span></span>那么莫英便也是鬼月至阴时辰生人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>至阴之血可引纯阳<span><span>，</span></span>辅以珍稀<span><span>，</span></span>施术炼制<span><span>，</span></span>能令病者愈<span><span>，</span></span>亡者生…</p>
 <p>原来<span><span>，</span></span>练诡术的不是鬼<span><span>，</span></span>而是人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>14<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>虽说我高度怀疑莫琼出于某种目的在修炼诡术<span><span>。</span></span>但地府向来只管死人的事不管活人的事<span><span>。</span></span>对我来说<span><span>，</span></span>抓住莫连风才是最关键的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>想着<span><span>，</span></span>我沉了口气<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你的问题我已经回答过了<span><span>。</span></span>那我的呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟好像很无奈<span><span>，</span></span>他极其轻微得叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>而后说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>说吧<span><span>，</span></span>你想知道什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>第一个问题<span><span>，</span></span>莫连风有没有什么珍贵的东西<span><span>，</span></span>应该在这雪桑谷中<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟轻笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这个问题莫琼已经回答过了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你就没有别的想说的<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我又问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟看着我<span><span>，</span></span>又笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你为什么对我小师父这么感兴趣<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我也笑了一下<span><span>，</span></span>但只是皮笑肉不笑<span><span>，</span></span>淡淡说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>如果我说这跟你弟弟的死有关<span><span>，</span></span>你会不会也同样感兴趣<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟蹙了蹙眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>什么意思<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没什么意思<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我看着秦一迟说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我答应帮你找出杀害你弟弟的人<span><span>。</span></span>作为交换<span><span>，</span></span>你也应该付出些什么<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟眼底闪过一抹光<span><span>，</span></span>嘴角微微动了一下<span><span>。</span></span>他说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姜叶颂啊姜叶颂<span><span>，</span></span>你还是和以前一样<span><span>，</span></span>冷漠…绝情<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>这么多年都没有变<span><span>，</span></span>不是很好么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我迎上秦一迟的目光<span><span>，</span></span>漠然补充道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还有<span><span>，</span></span>我现在叫林拂<span><span>，</span></span>袅袅林的林<span><span>，</span></span>拂生引的拂<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么林<span><span>？</span></span>什么拂<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟微微一怔<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不重要<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我抱臂看着秦一迟<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>秦一迟<span><span>，</span></span>我再问你一遍<span><span>，</span></span>关于莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>你究竟知道些什么<span><span>？</span></span>或者说你在隐瞒些什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我认识的那个秦一迟并非一个心里憋得住事的人<span><span>。</span></span>昔日雪桑谷中我们几个整日厮混<span><span>，</span></span>他竟从未提到过莫连风的事<span><span>，</span></span>可见他根本就是有心要隐瞒的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>果然秦一迟叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我不是要隐瞒…只是我不知道有些事说出来是好是坏<span><span>，</span></span>是对是错…还有…也不知该从何讲起<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你可以慢慢讲<span><span>。</span></span>还有<span><span>，</span></span>是好是坏<span><span>、</span></span>是对是错终究也不是由你决定<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我说罢<span><span>，</span></span>便静静等着秦一迟开口<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>过了好一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>他终于开始说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我九岁那年随父亲来雪桑谷拜访<span><span>，</span></span>无意间闯入了后山药阁<span><span>，</span></span>被谷中瘴气所伤<span><span>，</span></span>是莫连风救了我<span><span>。</span></span>我想拜他为师<span><span>，</span></span>他起初是不愿意的<span><span>。</span></span>后来经不住我日日往药阁跑<span><span>，</span></span>日日中瘴气<span><span>，</span></span>他终于心软将我留下<span><span>。</span></span>虽未正式说收我为徒<span><span>，</span></span>只称留下我整理医书和药材<span><span>，</span></span>可我日日所见所闻所感<span><span>，</span></span>皆是外面见不着<span><span>、</span></span>闻不到<span><span>、</span></span>也感受不了的稀奇古法与珍贵药材<span><span>。</span></span>嘴硬心软<span><span>，</span></span>我小师父就是这样的人<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>然后呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我追问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟的眉毛皱成了一团<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>其实那个时候我还很小…很多事也弄不清楚…只知道小师父似乎在找什么东西<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>他在找什么东西<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟欲言又止<span><span>，</span></span>上下抿了抿嘴唇<span><span>，</span></span>才说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>具体的我并不清楚…但我猜是药方…他每日都在药阁里不停折腾…比对药材…翻查藏书…一度达到近乎痴癫的地步<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>药方…<span><span>」</span></span> 我喃喃念叨<span><span>，</span></span>浑身不由自主打了个哆嗦<span><span>。</span></span>我抬眼盯着秦一迟<span><span>，</span></span>沉声问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你说他翻查藏书<span><span>？</span></span>可还记得都是些什么书<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟边回忆边说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>什么书都有…大多是药书古籍<span><span>，</span></span>还有…族谱和家书<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>族谱<span><span>？</span></span>家书<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我怔然张了张嘴<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这倒是出乎我的意料<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我问秦一迟道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那他有没有跟你提起过<span><span>，</span></span>他为何要找那东西<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>他没有说过<span><span>。</span></span>而且可能是心灰意冷了…后来他便不再找了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>活着时候遍寻谷中也找不到的东西…都放弃了的东西…为何死后还要找呢…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我喃喃自语<span><span>，</span></span>愁眉不展<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你说什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟忽然愣了一下<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没什么<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我敷衍道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你说…死了还要找<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟明显是听到了<span><span>。</span></span>他眼溜溜的眼睛直盯着我<span><span>，</span></span>阴森森问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你问了这么多我小师父的事<span><span>，</span></span>却一句也没有再提莫英<span><span>。</span></span>那只鬼<span><span>，</span></span>不是莫英<span><span>，</span></span>而是我小师父莫连风对不对<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>不得不说<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟很聪明<span><span>。</span></span>虽说年少时颇爱撒泼打滚<span><span>，</span></span>然脑子的的确确是几个人里最好用的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>事已至此<span><span>，</span></span>再瞒下去<span><span>，</span></span>倒显得刻意<span><span>。</span></span>于是我点了点头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟许久没有再说一个字<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我缓声道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你放心<span><span>，</span></span>你弟弟应该不是他害死的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你知道凶手是谁<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 秦一迟眼神如炬<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我没有说出我的推测<span><span>，</span></span>只是认真说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我不会妄下定论<span><span>。</span></span>一切还需要向莫连风求证<span><span>。</span></span>他自死后一直游荡在雪桑谷<span><span>，</span></span>也许知道干尸的真相<span><span>。</span></span>可是他现在躲起来了<span><span>，</span></span>昆仑的寻鬼术受药气影响施展不了<span><span>。</span></span>所以我要捏住他的命门<span><span>，</span></span>逼他现身才行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟狐疑地看着我<span><span>，</span></span>不知道在想些什么<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>为了让他放心<span><span>，</span></span>我便又道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>放心吧<span><span>。</span></span>不会让他魂飞魄散的<span><span>。</span></span>我是度他<span><span>，</span></span>不是害他<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>如果他乖乖听话<span><span>，</span></span>跟我回地府<span><span>，</span></span>自然不用魂飞魄散<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我如此腹诽<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我的话落地许久<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我相信你<span><span>。</span></span>何况我也想揪出害死阿行的罪魁祸首<span><span>。</span></span>可是…我对他的了解也就这么多<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>不等我开口<span><span>，</span></span>秦一迟又补充道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可我知道一个人<span><span>，</span></span>她应该很了解我小师父<span><span>。</span></span>只是这个人<span><span>，</span></span>你未必找得到<span><span>。</span></span>或者说<span><span>，</span></span>她是否还活着<span><span>，</span></span>我也不敢确定<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么人<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>文珠<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>文珠<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我蹙了蹙眉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>文珠姐姐是药阁的侍女<span><span>，</span></span>一直跟在我小师父身边<span><span>。</span></span>若说这谷里与我小师父最亲近的人<span><span>，</span></span>应该是她了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那她现在何处<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>听闻当年她回家省亲<span><span>，</span></span>便再未回来<span><span>。</span></span>此事我小师父还托了我父亲去江湖上打听<span><span>，</span></span>可惜<span><span>，</span></span>始终没有音讯<span><span>。</span></span>文珠说的那个村子根本就不存在<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫连风…拜托你父亲寻人<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我有些惊讶<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>秦一迟笑了<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是啊<span><span>，</span></span>鬼医莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>从不开口求人的<span><span>。</span></span>所以文珠姐姐对他来说<span><span>，</span></span>真的很重要<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>重要…重要…</p>
 <p>秦一迟的话提醒了我<span><span>。</span></span>也许是我先入为主<span><span>，</span></span>总觉得珍贵的一定是个物件儿<span><span>。</span></span>若莫连风要找的<span><span>，</span></span>或者说…要等的<span><span>，</span></span>不是个物件<span><span>，</span></span>而是一个人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我呼了口气<span><span>，</span></span>对秦一迟道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我出来很久了<span><span>，</span></span>苏温还在等我<span><span>。</span></span>我先回去了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>我便转过身去<span><span>。</span></span>然刚迈出两个台阶<span><span>，</span></span>就听见身后传来秦一迟的声音<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>诶…姜叶颂<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这一次我没有假装听不见<span><span>，</span></span>而是停下脚步<span><span>，</span></span>微微侧过头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>万事小心<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 他只说了这四个字<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>15<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>我回到房间的时候苏温还没回来<span><span>。</span></span>我便先行烧了纸回地府<span><span>，</span></span>询问一些事情<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这几日玉佩那边是一点动静也没有<span><span>。</span></span>阎王大人也不知道又去了哪里鬼混<span><span>。</span></span>自打鬼王回来<span><span>，</span></span>他便有意无意躲着鬼王似的<span><span>。</span></span>说不待见吧<span><span>，</span></span>当初还给人家鬼王办接风<span><span>。</span></span>说他怕鬼王吧<span><span>，</span></span>自打鬼王肃查地府<span><span>，</span></span>我也没少瞧见他偷偷翻白眼儿<span><span>。</span></span>所以我也想不通<span><span>，</span></span>他到底是怎么回事儿<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>地府给我回消息的时候<span><span>，</span></span>苏温正巧回来<span><span>。</span></span>我端着那黄纸还来不及看<span><span>，</span></span>便瞧见苏温一瘸一拐<span><span>，</span></span>拐进了屋来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你的腿…<span><span>」</span></span> 我蹙了蹙眉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温把剑放在了桌子上<span><span>，</span></span>自己给自己倒了一盏茶<span><span>，</span></span>便倒便说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可别提了…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>咕咚咕咚<span><span>，</span></span>苏温连喝了几大口早已冷了的茶<span><span>，</span></span>抹了抹嘴<span><span>，</span></span>继续说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>雪桑谷的后山竹林深处有处石门<span><span>，</span></span>我好不容易施术进去了<span><span>，</span></span>你猜怎么着<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>怎么着<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我来了精神<span><span>，</span></span>瞪大眼睛等着下文<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那里头有条狗<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温咧着嘴<span><span>，</span></span>一副不堪回首的模样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我想给他一杵子<span><span>，</span></span>但我怕他回去告我滥用职权打压下属<span><span>。</span></span>于是我只能强忍着<span><span>，</span></span>问他<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>一条狗<span><span>，</span></span>然后呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>然后我就回来了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温摸了摸自己的心脏<span><span>，</span></span>云淡风轻<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>它咬你了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我咬牙问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>吓都给我吓死了<span><span>。</span></span>我是拔腿就跑<span><span>，</span></span>可能跑得太快…有点儿抽筋儿<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>抽…<span><span>」</span></span> 我额上三道黑线<span><span>，</span></span>一拳头锤在桌面上<span><span>，</span></span>不可置信得盯着苏温<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>一条狗<span><span>？</span></span>一条狗就给你吓回来了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温一脸惊愕<span><span>，</span></span>对我道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那可不是一般的狗<span><span>，</span></span>它比人还高<span><span>，</span></span>比狮子还壮<span><span>，</span></span>有九个脑袋<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span><span>，</span></span>苏温伸出手指<span><span>，</span></span>比了个<span><span>「</span></span>七<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>九个脑袋…<span><span>」</span></span> 我微微愣了一下<span><span>，</span></span>即刻又问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你有注意它的爪子么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我正要说这个<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温宛如遇到知己<span><span>，</span></span>凑得又近了些<span><span>，</span></span>神神秘秘道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那狗每只爪子上竟然有二十几根指头<span><span>！</span></span>二十…几来着…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温在心里数着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我倒吸了一口凉气<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>二十四…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>对<span><span>！</span></span>二十四<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温拍了拍桌子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>诶…<span><span>？</span></span>大人你怎么知道它是二十四指…<span><span>」</span></span> 苏温大大的眼睛大大的疑惑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我没理他<span><span>，</span></span>沉浸在自己的惊愕之中<span><span>，</span></span>喃喃念叨道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>nüè…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>长得是挺虐的…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我叹了口气<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是䖋…我说那大狗的名字是䖋<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span><span>，</span></span>我给苏温写了下来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温看着那字蹙了蹙眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这破名字<span><span>，</span></span>该不会又是异诡阁起的吧<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>谁起的我倒是不知道…但这东西一直守在袅袅林中<span><span>，</span></span>是袅袅林的最后一道关卡<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温可是有理有据了<span><span>，</span></span>此时又拍了拍桌子<span><span>，</span></span>腰板儿也挺直了不少<span><span>，</span></span>振振道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你看看<span><span>，</span></span>袅袅林的最后一道关卡<span><span>，</span></span>我过不去是不是很正常<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温话音刚落<span><span>，</span></span>神色却变了<span><span>。</span></span>他看着我<span><span>，</span></span>蹙眉问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>袅袅林的凶兽<span><span>，</span></span>为什么出现在这儿<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我亦百思不得其解<span><span>，</span></span>于是只能摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不知道…我知道那个石门后面一定是有什么不可告人的秘密<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温想了想<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>既然是袅袅林里的东西<span><span>，</span></span>大人你应该知道怎么过关的<span><span>。</span></span>不如…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他话没说完就被我一泼冷水给浇醒了<span><span>。</span></span>我幽幽说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你有所不知<span><span>。</span></span>这袅袅林里的䖋和押魂使之间是有血契的<span><span>，</span></span>每个押魂使都有对应的一头䖋<span><span>，</span></span>而那头䖋也只听它契主的召唤<span><span>。</span></span>所以单独的一个押魂使绝不可能进入袅袅林<span><span>，</span></span>必须要五个押魂使一起<span><span>，</span></span>五头守着最后关卡的䖋才会全部放行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>所以你们五个<span><span>，</span></span>互相配合<span><span>，</span></span>也互相牵制<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我<span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>」</span></span>了一声儿<span><span>，</span></span>又道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不止我们<span><span>，</span></span>历代的押魂使皆是如此<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温蹙眉问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可…现在地府的押魂使不是只剩下你和檀逢大人了么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我给苏温解释道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>虽说如此<span><span>，</span></span>可他们三个的血契并没有解除<span><span>。</span></span>若要进入袅袅林的最深处<span><span>，</span></span>还是需要他们的配合<span><span>。</span></span>不过…如今地府已经在选拔新的押魂使<span><span>，</span></span>等新官上任<span><span>，</span></span>原有的血契解除<span><span>，</span></span>他们便会有新的契主<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温想了想<span><span>，</span></span>又说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可是…如果袅袅林只有五头䖋<span><span>，</span></span>那这一头必然是你们其中之一的契兽<span><span>。</span></span>不若问问其他几位大人<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我叹了口气<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>离开地府前<span><span>，</span></span>我才巡查过袅袅林…那五头䖋都在那里守着<span><span>，</span></span>这个<span><span>，</span></span>不属于我们任何一个<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那要不要再给异诡阁烧信问问<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>先不用<span><span>。</span></span>如果那石门背后真有什么至关重要的<span><span>，</span></span>我可能要亲自回趟地府<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>我又问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>除了这个<span><span>，</span></span>可有别的收获<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温老实说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>鬼呢<span><span>，</span></span>是半只都没找到<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我浑身一瘫<span><span>，</span></span>差点倒在桌前<span><span>，</span></span>对苏温这鬼小子<span><span>，</span></span>我就不该有所期待<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>岂料<span><span>，</span></span>苏温大喘气儿<span><span>，</span></span>还藏了一手<span><span>。</span></span>只听他幽幽道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>但我打听到一件事儿<span><span>，</span></span>雪桑谷近十年来偶尔会有人失踪<span><span>。</span></span>我怀疑他们被抓去做了药引<span><span>。</span></span>于是我给地府烧信要了近十年的雪桑谷死簿<span><span>，</span></span>那几位<span><span>，</span></span>的确是血尽而死<span><span>，</span></span>且是至阴时辰生人<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>厉害啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我看着苏温<span><span>，</span></span>笑了一下<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>等等…失踪<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我忽然想起一个人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>死簿还在你手里么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>从衣服里掏出了一张纸<span><span>，</span></span>平放在了桌子上<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我仔仔细细看了过去<span><span>，</span></span>一遍又一遍<span><span>，</span></span>却没找到文珠的名字<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人你在找什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>还记得后山的药阁么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我抬眼瞧着苏温<span><span>，</span></span>压着嗓子问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温又点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>莫连风生前常去的地方<span><span>，</span></span>之前也都布过苦陀铃的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我觉得他就在那儿<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>在苏温疑惑的神色下<span><span>，</span></span>我给他重新讲了一遍从秦一迟处打探来的消息<span><span>，</span></span>关于莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>也关于文珠<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我以为苏温会关心莫连风翻遍古籍究竟在找什么<span><span>，</span></span>再不济也会关心文珠是谁<span><span>？</span></span>为什么失踪<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>可苏温的关注点却异常清奇<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人…你露馅儿了…<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 他非常真挚<span><span>，</span></span>又略带无语地看着我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我…<span><span>」</span></span> 我嘎巴了两下嘴<span><span>，</span></span>也反驳不了他<span><span>。</span></span>只能剜了他一眼<span><span>，</span></span>道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我说了我是昆仑的人<span><span>，</span></span>这怎么说也不算彻底露馅儿吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温撇了撇嘴<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>他既能猜到莫英早就死了<span><span>，</span></span>也能猜到那鬼是莫连风<span><span>。</span></span>你觉得…他会信你的鬼话<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我…鬼…<span><span>」</span></span> 我伸出手指<span><span>，</span></span>支吾了许久<span><span>，</span></span>终究还是无言以对<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温这鬼小子<span><span>，</span></span>干啥啥不行<span><span>，</span></span>说话倒是一个顶仨<span><span>。</span></span>回到地府说啥我也给他整到谈判队里去<span><span>。</span></span>下回再跟九重天交涉<span><span>，</span></span>放出我们苏温<span><span>，</span></span>一定咬得他们哑口无言<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>咳咳…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>想着<span><span>，</span></span>我挑了挑眉<span><span>，</span></span>露出奸笑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>！</span></span>你还有脸笑<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温蹙眉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我…脸…<span><span>」</span></span> 我一拍桌子<span><span>，</span></span>怒目圆睁<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>苏温<span><span>，</span></span>我给你脸了是吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这才几日<span><span>，</span></span>苏温这鬼小子竟然丝毫不怕我了<span><span>，</span></span>称呼也从您彻底变成了你<span><span>。</span></span>此刻他掏了掏耳朵<span><span>，</span></span>极其敷衍得安抚我道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>我只是提醒你<span><span>，</span></span>小心那个秦一迟<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我正气极<span><span>，</span></span>苏温跟个没事鬼一样<span><span>，</span></span>接着说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>如大人所说<span><span>，</span></span>过几日便是莫连风的冥诞<span><span>，</span></span>那么<span><span>，</span></span>莫连风的生辰便不是鬼月至阴时辰…他不是死于诡术<span><span>，</span></span>他可能真的如莫琼所说<span><span>，</span></span>是病死的<span><span>。</span></span>那那个文珠呢<span><span>？</span></span>为何突然就失踪了<span><span>？</span></span>难不成…她也成了干尸了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我摇了摇头<span><span>，</span></span>指了指桌子上雪桑谷十年死簿<span><span>。</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>她的名字不在上面<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温忽然抱起胳膊<span><span>，</span></span>盯着我看<span><span>，</span></span>看得我浑身发毛<span><span>，</span></span>甚至还有那么一丢丢的害羞<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温这鬼小子<span><span>，</span></span>小模样儿还挺好看<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>若放在以前<span><span>，</span></span>九重天与地府不合那几年<span><span>，</span></span>送去和亲也是极好的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>想着<span><span>，</span></span>我又露出奸笑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人…大…人…大人<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温忽然大喊<span><span>，</span></span>吓我一跳<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>还是别送去九重天了<span><span>。</span></span>就他这大嗓门儿<span><span>，</span></span>在清净的九重天<span><span>，</span></span>不到三天<span><span>，</span></span>就得被送回来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>怎么了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你手里的那一团是什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我蹙了蹙眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>什么一团…是信<span><span>！</span></span>你回来时候我正要看地府的回信<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦…<span><span>」</span></span> 苏温笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可是地府的信马上就要让你揉碎了…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span><span>，</span></span>苏温指了指我紧攥的手<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我低头一看<span><span>，</span></span>好家伙<span><span>。</span></span>好好的一张纸<span><span>，</span></span>让我给揉成了团<span><span>，</span></span>中间还露了几个窟窿<span><span>。</span></span></p>
