 <p><span><span>「</span></span>地府这纸<span><span>，</span></span>质量也不咋地啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我咳嗽了两声儿<span><span>，</span></span>慢慢展开手里皱巴巴的纸<span><span>，</span></span>尴尬得抖了几抖<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>看着那信<span><span>，</span></span>我微微张开了嘴<span><span>，</span></span>喉咙一哽<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>看来…我必须回趟地府了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温好奇凑了过来<span><span>。</span></span>那异诡阁的骆无极吝啬言语<span><span>，</span></span>纸上只写了断断续续的一行字<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p>编号 0577<span><span>，</span></span>任务失败<span><span>，</span></span>现服刑于灵幽台<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温见字<span><span>，</span></span>骤然严肃起来<span><span>，</span></span>皱眉望向我<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>你问了什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我问了文珠是否已经死了…地府有没有她的消息…<span><span>」</span></span> 我忽然有些恍惚<span><span>，</span></span>冰冷之感骤涌于头顶<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我深深吸了口气<span><span>，</span></span>抬头看着苏温道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>编号 0577<span><span>，</span></span>文珠是名鬼差<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>16<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>彼时<span><span>，</span></span>看着那回信<span><span>，</span></span>我十分震惊<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温看着我<span><span>，</span></span>眼睛微微睁大<span><span>，</span></span>指着那信<span><span>，</span></span>冷幽幽问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>地府的鬼差犯了错大多降职<span><span>，</span></span>重一些的革职投胎<span><span>，</span></span>即便去玉露池都是罕见<span><span>。</span></span>她究竟犯了什么大错<span><span>，</span></span>竟要去灵幽台燃烛三百年<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我叹了口气<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>灵幽台有去无回<span><span>。</span></span>我必须立刻返回地府想办法见她<span><span>。</span></span>我走的期间若有人找我<span><span>，</span></span>拖着些便是<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>于是<span><span>，</span></span>我回到了地府<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>灵幽台虽说不属于什么禁地<span><span>，</span></span>但地府诸鬼一般也都不会去那儿触霉头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我徘徊在灵幽台外<span><span>，</span></span>按理说这里由鬼卫负责<span><span>，</span></span>我应该直接去找他们<span><span>。</span></span>然自打鬼王肃查地府<span><span>，</span></span>原有的情面是统统没有了<span><span>。</span></span>用檀逢的话说<span><span>，</span></span>那就是<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p>押魂使的面子还不如那刚纳好的鞋底子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我正琢磨着<span><span>，</span></span>忽然有个鬼差喊我名字<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可是林拂林大人<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你找我<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>鬼差谄媚得笑了笑<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是异诡阁骆大人找您<span><span>。</span></span>他说见着您<span><span>，</span></span>便告诉您他在异诡阁六层等着<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极这老贼<span><span>，</span></span>是摸准了我一定会回来的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>行了我知道了<span><span>。</span></span>劳烦了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我提剑拱了拱手<span><span>，</span></span>便抬腿往异诡阁去了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>刚进异诡阁<span><span>，</span></span>我就被一股子浓烟差点给熏出来<span><span>。</span></span>要说这异诡阁我也来过几次<span><span>，</span></span>然这第一层我就没有一次不是捏着鼻子进去的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>异诡阁的第一层<span><span>，</span></span>九九八十一根檀香<span><span>，</span></span>终年不断香火<span><span>，</span></span>供奉诸佛<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一群鬼<span><span>，</span></span>整日烧香拜佛<span><span>，</span></span>你敢信<span><span>？</span></span>就连那九天外大慈大悲的佛祖估计都不敢信<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>异诡阁的第六层<span><span>，</span></span>都是些奇书杂卷<span><span>，</span></span>有异诡阁的鬼侍带着我七拐八拐来到了骆无极所在之处<span><span>。</span></span>我踏进门时骆无极正端坐在正中央的案前<span><span>，</span></span>闻声抬头<span><span>，</span></span>不怀好意得对我笑了笑<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>林大人<span><span>，</span></span>好久不见了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>为什么找我<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我其实有点儿明知故问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>因为我觉得你需要找我<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我盯着他<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>骆大人知道如何进灵幽台<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极笑了<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>灵幽台如今你是进不去了<span><span>，</span></span>不过你可以告诉我你到底想知道些什么<span><span>。</span></span>也许我可以发发善心告诉你也说不定<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你知道文珠的事<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我依旧半信半疑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极手中摆弄着一块奇形怪状的石头<span><span>，</span></span>口中幽幽说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>文珠以前在异诡阁当差<span><span>，</span></span>你说我知不知道<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我蹙眉打量着骆无极<span><span>，</span></span>此刻他正翘个二郎腿<span><span>，</span></span>似笑非笑地看着我<span><span>。</span></span>瞧他那模样我便知道<span><span>，</span></span>他又在打什么坏主意<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你想干什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我眯了眯眼睛<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>帮你啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 他笑道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我哼了一声儿<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我是说<span><span>，</span></span>你想从我这儿得到什么<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我要你帮我个小忙 很小很小的小忙<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>骆无极眼里透着精光<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>您还真是无利不起早啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我假笑着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极敷衍得拱了拱手<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>过奖过奖<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>说吧<span><span>，</span></span>什么忙<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不急不急<span><span>，</span></span>你先应下<span><span>，</span></span>等雪桑谷一事完结<span><span>，</span></span>你再帮我<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我狐疑得看了他一眼<span><span>。</span></span>虽说我总觉得事情没他说得那么简单<span><span>，</span></span>然我倒也不信他骆无极敢提出什么出格的要求<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我答应你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极伸出手<span><span>，</span></span>笑看着我<span><span>。</span></span>极不情愿得<span><span>，</span></span>我走过去与他击了掌<span><span>。</span></span>而后便问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>掌也击过了<span><span>，</span></span>现在你可以说了么<span><span>？</span></span>文珠当初执行的是什么任务<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极伸了个懒腰<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>当年异诡阁的卷宗有一部分的誊抄本遗落在外<span><span>，</span></span>她是去销毁誊抄本的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我愣住了<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>誊抄本<span><span>？</span></span>地府的东西为何阳间会有誊抄本<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>这可就说来话长了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极看着我<span><span>，</span></span>极其古怪得笑了一下<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>三千年前<span><span>，</span></span>地府有个押魂使偷偷誊抄了其中一卷<span><span>，</span></span>在阳间修炼诡术<span><span>，</span></span>致使那一卷的誊抄本一直流落阳间<span><span>。</span></span>我们找了她好多年<span><span>，</span></span>好不容易有了线索<span><span>，</span></span>文珠被派上去执行这个任务<span><span>，</span></span>可她却失败了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>押魂使<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我大惊失色<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你是说地府的押魂使在阳间修炼诡术<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>就在雪桑谷中<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极点了点头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>胆大包天…<span><span>」</span></span> 我喉咙一哽<span><span>，</span></span>几乎说不出话来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我一直以为我的胆子已经够大了<span><span>，</span></span>虽说整日吵吵着让那些鬼魂飞魄散<span><span>，</span></span>然真正这么做的<span><span>，</span></span>三千年来也不过就那么几次<span><span>。</span></span>这个押魂使真的可以用胆大妄为来形容了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那头䖋…<span><span>」</span></span> 我忽然反应过来<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>苏温在雪桑谷后山看到了一头䖋<span><span>，</span></span>似乎在守着什么东西<span><span>。</span></span>所以那头䖋<span><span>，</span></span>就是当初那个押魂使带走的契兽<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大概是吧<span><span>。</span></span>具体情况是怎么样的也只有文珠知道<span><span>。</span></span>可她的嘴很严<span><span>，</span></span>很多事直到她被送去灵幽台也没有说<span><span>。</span></span> <span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我蹙了蹙眉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>任务失败…还缄口不言…文珠她…也在守护那石门背后的秘密么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我想不通<span><span>，</span></span>紧接着问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可即便文珠任务失败<span><span>，</span></span>也不至于要去灵幽台<span><span>。</span></span>究竟是为什么她要领如此重的责罚<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极幽幽道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>因为她背叛地府<span><span>，</span></span>不仅没有拿回誊抄本<span><span>，</span></span>还告诉了他另一半的秘密<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>他…<span><span>」</span></span> 我盯着骆无极<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>谁<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>其实我心里已经有了答案<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极咧了咧嘴角<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>莫连风<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我呼了口气<span><span>，</span></span>又问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你说的另一半的秘密<span><span>，</span></span>是什么意思<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>昔日那个押魂使只留下了一半药方<span><span>，</span></span>都是些阳间能寻到的<span><span>。</span></span>不好找<span><span>，</span></span>可终归是找得到<span><span>。</span></span>可有一副不寻常的药引她没有留下<span><span>。</span></span>少了这味药引<span><span>，</span></span>本可相安无事<span><span>，</span></span>可文珠泄露了出去<span><span>，</span></span>将埋下的祸根彻底拔了出来<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>药方…药引…<span><span>」</span></span> 我喃喃重复着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极鬼笑了一下<span><span>，</span></span>伸出手指隔空点了点<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你应该已经想到了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我倒吸了一口冷气<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span><span><span>《</span></span>十三凶煞•拂生引<span><span>》</span></span>…那个押魂使当年从异诡阁誊抄的走的…是愈生还阳之术…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不错<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>至阴之血可引纯阳<span><span>。</span></span>这个药引那个押魂使没有留下<span><span>，</span></span>可文珠背叛地府<span><span>，</span></span>扰乱了阳间秩序<span><span>。</span></span>你觉得她难道不应该被送到灵幽台么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>难道莫连风也在练诡术么…可是分明是…<span><span>」</span></span> 我实在想不通<span><span>，</span></span>话说一半就不说了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可分明是莫琼<span><span>，</span></span>是么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极好似我肚子里的蛔虫<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我点了点头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>据文珠所说<span><span>，</span></span>莫连风因为始终无法狠下心去取人性命<span><span>，</span></span>最终还是放弃了这种诡术<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我想了想<span><span>，</span></span>又问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我有一个问题…至阴之血而已<span><span>，</span></span>取便取了<span><span>，</span></span>定要取到要人性命的地步么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>因为这味药引才是这诡术的重头戏<span><span>，</span></span>少量的血根本起不到任何作用<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极边说着<span><span>，</span></span>边搓着手里那块早就被摸得光华的古怪石头<span><span>。</span></span>我不得不强迫自己把注意力从那石头上转移出来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我叹了口气<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那昔日那个押魂使<span><span>，</span></span>只留下普通的药方<span><span>，</span></span>而没留下这最重要的药引<span><span>，</span></span>也是因为觉得太过残忍么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极笑了<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>残忍<span><span>？</span></span>昔日她从地府逃走<span><span>，</span></span>躲在雪桑谷修炼诡术<span><span>，</span></span>多少人死在她的手里<span><span>。</span></span>她怕地府发现<span><span>，</span></span>滥用押魂之术<span><span>，</span></span>使那些鬼魂被封于雪桑谷中几十年<span><span>，</span></span>直到她身死<span><span>，</span></span>才得以往生<span><span>。</span></span>临终前她虽销毁了那个药引的记载<span><span>，</span></span>然不过是想为后世子孙累积福报<span><span>。</span></span>这点儿善意<span><span>，</span></span>本就是残忍的一部分<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>等等…<span><span>」</span></span> 我眉头紧锁<span><span>，</span></span>一眼不眨得盯着骆无极<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你刚刚说'身死'<span><span>？</span></span>她不是押魂使么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极眼里透着幽光<span><span>，</span></span>复露出那似笑非笑的诡异表情来<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不然你以为她修炼的是什么<span><span>？</span></span>想得到的又是什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>紧接着<span><span>，</span></span>骆无极阴沉沉道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还阳之术<span><span>，</span></span>那个押魂使<span><span>，</span></span>成功了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不可能…<span><span>」</span></span> 我打了个寒战<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这世上<span><span>，</span></span>谁都不可能逆转阴阳<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极懒散道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没什么不可能<span><span>。</span></span>我异诡阁的卷宗<span><span>，</span></span>没有一份是假的<span><span>。</span></span>何况…这诡术<span><span>，</span></span>在她之后还成功过一次<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我心里一沉<span><span>，</span></span>想到一个人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那个皇帝…<span><span>」</span></span> 我喃喃说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温说过<span><span>，</span></span>三千年前有个皇帝痴迷这种邪术<span><span>，</span></span>遍寻天下奇人异士为其炼制丹药<span><span>，</span></span>最后真的成功了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我以为那只是个传说<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极哼笑<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>所谓传说<span><span>，</span></span>皆是打着虚幻幌子的真实<span><span>。</span></span>林拂<span><span>，</span></span>你做鬼差三千年<span><span>，</span></span>做押魂使也有七八百年<span><span>。</span></span>这个道理<span><span>，</span></span>你还不明白么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>紧接着<span><span>，</span></span>骆无极忽然问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你不想知道那个押魂使叫什么名字么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么名字<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>殷如惜<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>殷如惜…</p>
 <p>我心头一紧<span><span>，</span></span>这名字听着<span><span>，</span></span>倒是有些耳熟<span><span>。</span></span>可我却一时想不起在何处听到过<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极看着我<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你还记得她么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我盯着骆无极的眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>幽幽道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>她做押魂使的时候我只是个小鬼差<span><span>，</span></span>按理说我应该没见过她<span><span>。</span></span>或者说<span><span>，</span></span>我应该记得她么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>古怪得扯了扯嘴角<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你会记起她的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>如此吊人胃口的话<span><span>，</span></span>也就他骆无极能说得出来<span><span>。</span></span>不过要让他失望了<span><span>，</span></span>我并不感兴趣<span><span>。</span></span>现在我只想完成任务<span><span>，</span></span>赶紧回到地府<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>于是我问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>还有一个问题<span><span>。</span></span>莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>他究竟是不是在等文珠<span><span>。</span></span>他知道文珠是鬼差么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>他不知道文珠的身份<span><span>，</span></span>不然也就不会到处托人去找了<span><span>。</span></span>但他究竟是不是因为在等文珠而不肯走…就要你自己参悟了<span><span>。</span></span>毕竟…莫英也没告诉我<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫…<span><span>」</span></span> 我震惊得张了张嘴<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你说莫英<span><span>？</span></span>他死后来过你这儿<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极极其无语地看着我<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不然你以为我异诡阁是如何延续至今的<span><span>？</span></span>那可有一大部分是我们一点点一点点从那些鬼的嘴里抠出来的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>低级…<span><span>」</span></span> 我十分嫌弃<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>真没想到<span><span>，</span></span>堂堂异诡阁<span><span>，</span></span>竟靠这种方式挖消息<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>等等…再等等…</p>
 <p>我抬起头<span><span>，</span></span>阴森得看向骆无极<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你的意思是<span><span>，</span></span>你早知道那鬼就是莫连风<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那又如何<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极毫无愧意<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我气得攥了攥手中的剑<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那你不早说<span><span>！</span></span>我和苏温白费了多少工夫你知不知道<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>还有<span><span>，</span></span>地府还要拉着张大脸去问录命司<span><span>，</span></span>你有没有心<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我如此激动<span><span>，</span></span>骆无极却异常平静<span><span>。</span></span>他轻轻笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>林拂<span><span>，</span></span>你是傻了么<span><span>？</span></span>你该不会忘了<span><span>，</span></span>异诡阁的规矩是不问不答<span><span>。</span></span>即便是阎王<span><span>，</span></span>也不例外<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>规矩…异诡阁都是鬼才<span><span>，</span></span>都是鬼才啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我插着腰<span><span>，</span></span>气得点了点头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>过奖过奖<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极再一次敷衍得拱手致谢<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我伸出手指<span><span>，</span></span>隔空狠狠点了点骆无极<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>还有<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极笑了一下<span><span>，</span></span>十分神秘得从旁边桌子上拿起一张黄纸<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>恭喜你解锁一个新任务<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我怀疑我是糊涂了<span><span>，</span></span>出现了幻听<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极笑道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>鬼王大人说了<span><span>，</span></span>若你来问文珠的事<span><span>，</span></span>便要你一并将她未完成的任务也给结了<span><span>。</span></span>销毁誊抄本<span><span>，</span></span>全部<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>黄纸自他指尖飞旋<span><span>，</span></span>飘到了我面前<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我接下黄纸<span><span>，</span></span>几乎已经按捺不住撕碎鬼王的一颗躁动的心<span><span>，</span></span>咬着牙道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>鬼王大人为何要把任务下给你<span><span>，</span></span>而不直接给我<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦…<span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极相当淡定<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可能他不想见到你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>17<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>异诡阁内<span><span>，</span></span>我端着那鬼王新下的任务<span><span>，</span></span>七窍生烟<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我努力平静地看着骆无极<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>雪桑谷后山的石门里到底隐藏着什么秘密<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极笑道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这个我是真的不知道<span><span>。</span></span>可是我猜…誊抄本可能就在那里面<span><span>，</span></span>莫连风…可能也在那里面<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你的意思是若想销毁那个誊抄本<span><span>，</span></span>抓住莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>就必须得那头䖋放我过石门才行<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那是最直接的办法<span><span>。</span></span>但我劝你还是试试别的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>为什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我蹙了蹙眉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>为什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我说过<span><span>，</span></span>当初的那个押魂使还了阳<span><span>，</span></span>如今已经死了不知多少年<span><span>。</span></span>那契兽早就易主<span><span>，</span></span>现今那血契在谁身上<span><span>，</span></span>异诡阁也不知道<span><span>。</span></span>不过…如果你是殷如惜<span><span>，</span></span>你如果要留那凶兽为你看家护院<span><span>，</span></span>你会把新的血契缔结在谁的身上<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>如果我是她…<span><span>」</span></span> 我思量着<span><span>，</span></span>口中喃喃<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我的孩子…或者说…后人<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不错<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>结合文珠三缄其口的状态<span><span>，</span></span>我觉得现今那䖋的契主<span><span>，</span></span>应该是莫连风<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>这不是个死循环么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我微微摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>如果莫连风在石门后面<span><span>，</span></span>如何能让他出来<span><span>，</span></span>召唤凶兽<span><span>，</span></span>打开石门<span><span>。</span></span>这是根本不可能的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极扬起嘴角<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我的猜测已经告诉你了<span><span>，</span></span>至于办法就要你自己想了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我有那么一会儿没有说话<span><span>，</span></span>而后沉着声音问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>如果没有血契…降伏䖋的可能性有多大<span><span>？</span></span>异诡阁有什么方法么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我在地府这么久<span><span>，</span></span>从未见过有谁能够绕过没有血契的䖋<span><span>，</span></span>进入他们所看守的地方<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我攥了攥拳头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那岂不是…永远也进不去那石门了<span><span>？</span></span>莫连风怎么会蠢到自己走出来<span><span>，</span></span>再领我们进去<span><span>？</span></span>这次的任务…分明是那…是那…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>分明是那鬼王给我下的一个绊脚石<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我如此腹诽<span><span>，</span></span>嘴巴开了又闭<span><span>，</span></span>终究没有说出口<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那边骆无极就像看透了我的心思<span><span>，</span></span>轻笑了一声儿<span><span>，</span></span>而后微微仰起头<span><span>，</span></span>幽幽说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>总之<span><span>，</span></span>没有人能够降伏没有血契的䖋<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说罢<span><span>，</span></span>他似乎忽然想到什么<span><span>，</span></span>眯了眯眼睛<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>倒也不是没有<span><span>。</span></span>只是那是几万年前的事了<span><span>，</span></span>那时候地府还不叫地府<span><span>，</span></span>而叫冥府<span><span>。</span></span>曾有一只鬼徒手斩杀了三头看守重犯的䖋<span><span>，</span></span>虽说身受重伤<span><span>，</span></span>但的确是做到了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>谁<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极看着我的眼睛幽深透亮<span><span>，</span></span>一字一字沉沉说道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>昔日幽冥十三凶煞之首<span><span>，</span></span>龙阁帝鸢<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>帝鸢…<span><span>」</span></span> 我倒吸了一口凉气<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>所以我说<span><span>，</span></span>劝你试试别的办法<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极说罢<span><span>，</span></span>伸了个懒腰<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>话已言尽<span><span>，</span></span>也到了骆某休息的时候了<span><span>。</span></span>林大人<span><span>，</span></span>慢走不送<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span><span>，</span></span>冲门口比了个让的手势<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我转身出门前<span><span>，</span></span>忽然又想到一件事<span><span>。</span></span>于是停下来<span><span>，</span></span>回过头看着骆无极道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我还有一个问题<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极静静看着我<span><span>，</span></span>似乎在等着我开口<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那个还了阳的押魂使<span><span>，</span></span>死后去了哪里<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>投胎去了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 骆无极说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我有些惊讶<span><span>，</span></span>问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>地府没有责罚她么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极笑道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>她还了阳<span><span>，</span></span>就是凡人<span><span>。</span></span>以凡人之躯身死来到地府<span><span>，</span></span>又如何再以押魂使的身份去惩罚她呢<span><span>？</span></span>地府没有这样的规矩<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我哼了一声儿<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>又是规矩…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极幽幽道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>话虽如此<span><span>，</span></span>可是她的后人一直都在受着责罚<span><span>，</span></span>也算是她背弃地府<span><span>，</span></span>逆转阴阳的代价吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>后人…<span><span>」</span></span> 我蹙眉念着<span><span>，</span></span>忽然好像明白了<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>雪桑谷…她在雪桑谷修炼诡术<span><span>，</span></span>她是雪桑谷的人<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>骆无极点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那押魂使就是雪桑谷第一任谷主的夫人<span><span>，</span></span>殷如惜<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>18<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>我回到雪桑谷的时候已是夜里<span><span>。</span></span>苏温一直在我房间里等着<span><span>。</span></span>我推门进去的时候<span><span>，</span></span>他的身子坐得挺直<span><span>，</span></span>正端着一盏茶<span><span>，</span></span>微微侧过头来<span><span>，</span></span>我忽然一阵恍惚<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他很像我从前认识的某个人<span><span>。</span></span>可那人烂在记忆的最深处<span><span>，</span></span>千年而来<span><span>，</span></span>似乎只剩下了一个不清不楚的轮廓<span><span>。</span></span>如今<span><span>，</span></span>随便的什么人竟都能与他相似了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>想着<span><span>，</span></span>我暗自笑了一下<span><span>，</span></span>心中感触却不知是酸涩还是无奈<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>坐下后<span><span>，</span></span>苏温给我倒了茶<span><span>，</span></span>我喝了一口便开始讲在地府打听到的那些事<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一席话听罢<span><span>，</span></span>苏温蹙着眉<span><span>，</span></span>冷声说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不行<span><span>。</span></span>那帝鸢是什么人<span><span>，</span></span>你拿什么和她比<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我轻轻点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我知道<span><span>，</span></span>她能做到的我未必做得到<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>错<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温有些凶狠地盯着我<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你是一定做不到<span><span>！</span></span>所以别去送死<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我愤怒之余<span><span>，</span></span>有些感动<span><span>，</span></span>然感动之余<span><span>，</span></span>还有些无语<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>苏温<span><span>，</span></span>我是鬼<span><span>，</span></span>已经没有办法再死了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我半开玩笑道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可是苏温似乎很严肃<span><span>。</span></span>他的一双眼睛一直就没离开过我的双眼间<span><span>，</span></span>就那么看着我<span><span>，</span></span>微微闪烁<span><span>，</span></span>仿佛带着某种莫名的…恐惧<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>苏温…<span><span>」</span></span> 我抿了抿嘴唇<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>地府的差事<span><span>，</span></span>谁都拒绝不了<span><span>，</span></span>无论是我还是你<span><span>。</span></span>这个道理<span><span>，</span></span>你不会不明白<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温喉咙一哽<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可是…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没什么可是<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我坚决打断了苏温的话<span><span>，</span></span>沉沉道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我意已决<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>许久<span><span>，</span></span>苏温点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我跟你一起去<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不行<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我几乎拍案而起<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我尚没有胜算<span><span>，</span></span>你去了<span><span>，</span></span>便真的是自绝后路<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温十分平静地看着我<span><span>，</span></span>缓缓道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>若我不能去<span><span>，</span></span>你便也不能去<span><span>。</span></span>林大人<span><span>，</span></span>我知你奉命领三号牢房来阳间办差<span><span>。</span></span>但三号牢房自来是我说了算<span><span>，</span></span>过去如此<span><span>，</span></span>现在如此<span><span>，</span></span>往后亦如此<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>苏温你…<span><span>」</span></span> 我不解地看着苏温<span><span>。</span></span>那一瞬间<span><span>，</span></span>我觉得他无比陌生<span><span>，</span></span>同这些日子来我认识的那个苏温完全不同<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温沉了口气<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>放心<span><span>，</span></span>我会想办法把莫连风给引出来<span><span>，</span></span>总有办法结这个差事<span><span>，</span></span>不至于让三号牢房交不了差<span><span>，</span></span>也不至于让你我都丢了鬼命<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>引出来<span><span>？</span></span>你想怎么引…那…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我有些激动<span><span>，</span></span>可说着说着<span><span>，</span></span>我忽然给自己说通了<span><span>。</span></span>最开始<span><span>，</span></span>在我尚不知莫连风要等和要找的是一个人的时候<span><span>，</span></span>我就想着要用那东西引他出来的<span><span>。</span></span>而今却因一头䖋而横生枝节<span><span>，</span></span>倒是我想得愈发复杂了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我对苏温道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你说的对…引出来…如果莫连风真的是为了文珠才留在谷中<span><span>。</span></span>那么只要文珠回来<span><span>，</span></span>他便会现身<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温淡淡道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可真正的文珠回不来了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没错…<span><span>」</span></span> 我十分赞同得点了点头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>但是只要同地府要来画像<span><span>，</span></span>我们便可以有一个假文珠回来<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哪来的假…<span><span>」</span></span> 苏温说着<span><span>，</span></span>抬眸撞见了我诡异的眼神<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人…你…<span><span>」</span></span> 苏温的脚不安分得动了动<span><span>，</span></span>似乎想要逃跑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我一把按住他的肩膀<span><span>，</span></span>眯着眼阴森森道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>苏温乖<span><span>，</span></span>只要你好好扮成文珠<span><span>，</span></span>大人我不会亏待你的<span><span>。</span></span>以后啊<span><span>，</span></span>在三号牢房<span><span>，</span></span>还让你说了算<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>夜凉如水<span><span>，</span></span>冷风嗖嗖<span><span>。</span></span>苏温打了个喷嚏<span><span>，</span></span>因深感是自掘坟墓<span><span>，</span></span>终是一句话也没说出来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>19<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>文珠画像传回来的时候我还是有些惊讶的<span><span>。</span></span>文珠的样貌与我想象之中略微有些不同<span><span>。</span></span>之前想着<span><span>，</span></span>地府既派她上来接近莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>总归该是个风情万种的女鬼<span><span>，</span></span>稍微不济些<span><span>，</span></span>该有的明丽动人也须是有的<span><span>，</span></span>然却不想只是个瞧着年纪不大<span><span>，</span></span>勉强算作清秀的小丫头<span><span>，</span></span>唯有一处让人能多看几眼的<span><span>，</span></span>大概是那一对浅浅的梨窝<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温好信儿<span><span>，</span></span>凑过来看<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好看么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我抬眼问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温笑了笑<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没有大人好看<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看了苏温一眼<span><span>，</span></span>冷笑道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不用讨好我<span><span>。</span></span>凭你夸烂了你的嘴<span><span>，</span></span>媚瞎了你的眼<span><span>，</span></span>今日你也得给我扮成文珠<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不是…<span><span>」</span></span> 苏温忽然像是浑身散了架子<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>我堂堂一个男鬼<span><span>，</span></span>你怎么忍心让我扮成个女鬼<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你不扮谁扮<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我斜眼问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温吭哧起来<span><span>，</span></span>眼神闪烁<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那您…您…您自己…不成么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这会子求到我<span><span>，</span></span>称呼终于又从<span><span>「</span></span>你<span><span>」</span></span>变回<span><span>「</span></span>您<span><span>」</span></span>了<span><span>，</span></span>也没了方才那呵斥我时冷冰冰的嘴脸了<span><span>。</span></span>我笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span>又摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>小苏温<span><span>，</span></span>你也知道大人我脾气不太好<span><span>。</span></span>若是关键时候我受不了他在我面前哭天抢地<span><span>，</span></span>一个顺手让他魂飞魄散了<span><span>，</span></span>可怎么好<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温看着我<span><span>，</span></span>十分无语<span><span>。</span></span>但他心里一定也清楚<span><span>，</span></span>我并非是干不出那让莫连风魂飞魄散的事来<span><span>。</span></span>于是<span><span>，</span></span>号称在三号牢房说了算的苏温<span><span>，</span></span>不得不勉强应下了我的要求<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>入了夜<span><span>，</span></span>我跟这苏温来到后山<span><span>。</span></span>为免有人打扰<span><span>，</span></span>我在竹林外设下了鬼障<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>石门之外<span><span>，</span></span>我侧耳听了听<span><span>，</span></span>却什么动静也没听见<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>你真的确定莫连风在里面<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我压着嗓子道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>骆无极那老鬼<span><span>，</span></span>虽说瞧着不着调<span><span>。</span></span>但他的猜测<span><span>，</span></span>从来不是无根无据<span><span>。</span></span>他既这么说了<span><span>，</span></span>没有十成可能<span><span>，</span></span>最少也有八成<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温点了点头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>开石门<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>，</span></span>你真觉得这样有用么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>如果他真的在里面<span><span>，</span></span>就一定会出来<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温没再说什么<span><span>，</span></span>掌间运气<span><span>，</span></span>专心对付起那石门来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>就在那石门裂出一缕缝隙的时候<span><span>，</span></span>我听见了䖋喉咙里发出的轰隆响声<span><span>。</span></span>石门开到一半<span><span>，</span></span>那䖋的几个头明显已经陆续苏醒过来<span><span>，</span></span>瞪起血红的眼珠儿<span><span>，</span></span>似要扑食一般<span><span>。</span></span>极其迅速得<span><span>，</span></span>我指尖一弹<span><span>，</span></span>将那文珠的画像送进了石门之中<span><span>。</span></span>其实我也想过<span><span>，</span></span>那䖋会不会扑过去将画像咬得稀碎<span><span>。</span></span>但据我多年来在袅袅林中的观察<span><span>，</span></span>䖋这凶兽根本是个蠢兽<span><span>，</span></span>它只对血的味道敏感<span><span>，</span></span>身体里流淌着血的任何生物<span><span>，</span></span>哪怕是死了的鬼<span><span>，</span></span>它都会拼命撕咬<span><span>。</span></span>但是对于没有血气的所有东西却不见得多感兴趣<span><span>。</span></span>这也许就是袅袅林看守的漏洞<span><span>，</span></span>但我思虑了许多年<span><span>，</span></span>也没真正得试验过<span><span>。</span></span>而今看来<span><span>，</span></span>我猜得一点没错<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风出来的时候我与苏温已经等了许久<span><span>。</span></span>久到苏温酝酿好的感情都已经快要消耗干净了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>文珠<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风脸上的欣喜因为远处灼目的火光而骤然消失<span><span>。</span></span>他忽然停下脚步<span><span>，</span></span>警惕得看了眼四周<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>彼时<span><span>，</span></span>假文珠<span><span>，</span></span>也就是苏温<span><span>，</span></span>早已被我困在火圈之中<span><span>。</span></span>而我已然躲在暗处<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不要过来<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温大喊<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风眼露急色<span><span>，</span></span>说话的声音都在颤抖<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>文珠<span><span>，</span></span>不要怕<span><span>！</span></span>我来救你<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不要过来<span><span>，</span></span>昆仑的人在引你上钩<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温又是一声儿大喊<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>苏温这鬼小子临场发挥是真不错<span><span>。</span></span>莫连风此鬼极其狡猾<span><span>，</span></span>不演得逼真一些<span><span>，</span></span>他恐怕不会放下戒心<span><span>，</span></span>轻易相信一个失踪了十几年的人会忽然出现<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>如果你过来<span><span>，</span></span>我就死在这儿<span><span>！</span></span>快回石门后面去<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温泫然欲泣<span><span>，</span></span>明显又开始给自己加戏<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风身子微颤<span><span>，</span></span>眼里映着火光<span><span>，</span></span>攥了攥拳头<span><span>。</span></span>口中喃喃<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>昆仑的人<span><span>，</span></span>能奈我何<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他动作极快<span><span>，</span></span>虚影一般向苏温冲了过来<span><span>。</span></span>就在他刚刚接近火圈<span><span>，</span></span>我也准备好了随时出手的时候<span><span>，</span></span>他却忽然收回了已经伸出的手<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你不是文珠<span><span>！</span></span>你究竟谁<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫连风冷目灼灼<span><span>，</span></span>声音冰涩<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我是文珠啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温的声音带着哭腔<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你撒谎…文珠只有一个梨窝<span><span>，</span></span>而你是两个<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span><span>，</span></span>莫连风感觉到不对劲<span><span>，</span></span>转身就要往石门跑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>靠<span><span>！</span></span>我就说不能随便加戏<span><span>！</span></span>苏温这小子没事儿表演什么喜极而泣<span><span>！</span></span>简直偷鸡不成蚀把米<span><span>！</span></span>还有骆无极那个老贼<span><span>，</span></span>枉他号称天下第一聪明鬼<span><span>，</span></span>地府的大脑<span><span>，</span></span>异诡阁的心脏<span><span>。</span></span>就连人家文珠是几个梨窝<span><span>，</span></span>他都弄不清楚<span><span>！</span></span>我算明白了<span><span>，</span></span>这俩鬼完全就是我林拂攒修为之路上的绊脚石<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>此刻苏温已经追了过去<span><span>。</span></span>但眼见着他那小碎步<span><span>，</span></span>就没可能追上头也不回的莫连风<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>如果莫连风躲回石门后<span><span>，</span></span>再想让他出来<span><span>，</span></span>基本就不可能了<span><span>。</span></span>于是我阴森森眯了眯眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>从身侧悄然抽出了佩剑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>20<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫连风<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>彼时<span><span>，</span></span>我大喊了一声儿<span><span>，</span></span>右手运气<span><span>，</span></span>砰然关上了石门<span><span>。</span></span>左手扬手一个飞剑<span><span>，</span></span>眼见着那剑笔直向莫连风后脑勺追去<span><span>，</span></span>莫连风回头猛得一躲<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>此时我一把抓住了抛在半空的佩剑<span><span>，</span></span>又紧紧握回了手中<span><span>。</span></span>莫连风盯着我手中的剑<span><span>，</span></span>咬牙道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你不是昆仑的人<span><span>，</span></span>你是地府的鬼差<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>屁<span><span>！</span></span>我最恨别人说我是鬼差<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>在下地府押魂使林拂<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span><span>，</span></span>我腾然而起<span><span>，</span></span>自半空中向下将剑死死直插入莫连风的头中<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>大人<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 苏温忽然大喊<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我微微侧头<span><span>，</span></span>眼珠儿却盯着莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>回应苏温道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>放心<span><span>，</span></span>这点儿力度要不了他魂飞魄散<span><span>。</span></span>可再深半寸<span><span>，</span></span>我就不敢保证了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风被我这剑力逼着<span><span>，</span></span>扑通跪倒在地<span><span>，</span></span>发出震天悲鸣<span><span>。</span></span>只见他的额头骤然渗出许许多多汗珠儿<span><span>，</span></span>脸色惨白<span><span>，</span></span>一双眼睛极其怨愤地盯着我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我咬着后槽牙<span><span>，</span></span>冷眼盯着莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>一字一顿道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我问什么<span><span>，</span></span>你答什么<span><span>。</span></span>能做到你就眨眨眼<span><span>，</span></span>做不到我这手一抖<span><span>，</span></span>你也就解脱了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>尽管莫连风极其不情愿<span><span>，</span></span>但他终究还是眨了眨眼<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我心中哼笑<span><span>。</span></span>阎王大人说得对<span><span>，</span></span>人之所以好控制<span><span>，</span></span>就是因为欲望<span><span>，</span></span>难以割舍的欲望<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>第一个问题<span><span>，</span></span>莫英和莫琼的事你知道多少<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我知道莫英死了<span><span>，</span></span>莫琼顶替了他的位置<span><span>，</span></span>以他的身份活到现在<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我追问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那你应该在莫英死后见过他<span><span>。</span></span>他是死在他弟弟莫琼手里<span><span>，</span></span>对么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风看着我<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你既已经知道<span><span>，</span></span>又为何还要问我<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那我换个问题<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我冷冷问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>至阴之血<span><span>，</span></span>可引纯阳<span><span>。</span></span>莫英是至阴之血<span><span>，</span></span>秦一行是至阴之血<span><span>，</span></span>雪桑谷中无故失踪的人也都是至阴之血<span><span>。</span></span>然既你当年已经放弃这诡术<span><span>，</span></span>为何又会被莫琼知道<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这个问题你该去问他<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我眯了眯眼睛<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>文珠因为你而受灼魂噬魄之苦<span><span>，</span></span>而这雪桑谷每添一缕冤魂<span><span>，</span></span>便多增她一分业障<span><span>。</span></span>这就是你想要的结果么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风的眼睛忽然又亮了起来<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你说什么<span><span>？</span></span>文珠她怎么了<span><span>？</span></span>你真的见过文珠<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>笑道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不然你以为我哪里来的画像<span><span>？</span></span>不妨告诉你<span><span>，</span></span>昔日文珠为了你背叛地府<span><span>，</span></span>惹下天大祸事<span><span>，</span></span>如今去了一个比炼狱还要炼狱的地方<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>地府…她是地府的人…<span><span>」</span></span> 莫连风发疯了一般喃喃自语<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我早该想到的…我早该想到她并非一个普通人…能找到那药引的…怎么会是一个普通人…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>如果想救文珠<span><span>，</span></span>我劝你跟我合作<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你要我做什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫连风狐疑地盯着我<span><span>，</span></span>然眼神之中是难以掩藏的焦虑与担忧<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我问道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我想知道当年那个誊抄本<span><span>，</span></span>还有文珠给你的药引誊抄本<span><span>，</span></span>现在何处<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你想做什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫连风似乎很谨慎<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我奉地府之命<span><span>。</span></span>一是抓你回去<span><span>。</span></span>二是了结文珠未完成的任务<span><span>，</span></span>销毁誊抄本<span><span>，</span></span>终止这场人间灾祸<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风脸色苍白<span><span>，</span></span>嘴唇微微抖着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>如果你完成了<span><span>。</span></span>那文珠她会离开那个炼狱一样的地方么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不会<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我如实答道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我很想告诉他<span><span>，</span></span>会<span><span>。</span></span>可我不想违背自己的良心<span><span>。</span></span>许多年前<span><span>，</span></span>有人曾告诉我<span><span>，</span></span>虽身处幽暗<span><span>，</span></span>然应心向光明<span><span>，</span></span>只要心中有所坚守<span><span>，</span></span>便坦荡而无所畏惧<span><span>。</span></span>他那样的人<span><span>，</span></span>即便过了千年<span><span>，</span></span>可以依旧在人族的历史记忆中鲜活灿烂<span><span>，</span></span>一如当初<span><span>。</span></span>我曾一心想成为他那样的人<span><span>，</span></span>可惜千年来不过学到了皮毛<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>良心<span><span>，</span></span>可能是他唯一教会我的<span><span>，</span></span>而千年来仍没有被我忘记的东西<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>许久<span><span>，</span></span>我才渐渐缓过神来<span><span>。</span></span>看着莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>我缓缓说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>虽然她不会离开那里<span><span>。</span></span>但是至少她的业障不再增加<span><span>，</span></span>不会每一日<span><span>，</span></span>都比前一日过得更加痛苦<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风乌青的眼眶中溢出泪水<span><span>，</span></span>包裹着若隐若现的红血丝<span><span>，</span></span>许久没有说话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不知过了多久<span><span>，</span></span>我与他就这样僵持着<span><span>。</span></span>我没有再开口逼迫<span><span>，</span></span>因为我相信为了文珠<span><span>，</span></span>他一定会说<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>果然<span><span>，</span></span>过了一会儿<span><span>，</span></span>莫连风终于开了口<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>石门<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 他说道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>石门<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我蹙眉看着他<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你说誊抄本在石门后面<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风摇了摇头<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>只有一半在里面<span><span>。</span></span>文珠给我的那部分被我随着那场大火给烧了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你放那场火…是为了销毁关于药引的记载<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我犹疑问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我觉得不可思议<span><span>，</span></span>如此排场实在是有些大了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风叹息道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>昔日我为了找到药方<span><span>，</span></span>查遍古籍医书<span><span>，</span></span>写了很多笔记<span><span>。</span></span>我以为…<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风欲言又止<span><span>，</span></span>话锋明显一转<span><span>，</span></span>说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>总之我没有伤害任何人<span><span>，</span></span>文珠也没有<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我盯着莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>沉声道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你不杀伯仁<span><span>，</span></span>伯仁却因你而死<span><span>。</span></span>如果你当真销毁得彻底<span><span>，</span></span>莫琼又是如何发现这诡术背后的秘密的<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我不知道<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫连风脸色很难看<span><span>，</span></span>缓缓摇了摇头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>还有一个问题<span><span>。</span></span>你既然已经毁了文珠给你的那部分<span><span>，</span></span>为何不将剩下的誊抄本一并销毁<span><span>，</span></span>而是将它留在石门后<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我问道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风苦笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>将它留在那儿的不是我<span><span>。</span></span>若能销毁<span><span>，</span></span>我早便销毁了<span><span>。</span></span>只是那字刻在墙体中<span><span>，</span></span>早已成为莫家世世代代守护的秘密<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我眉头一紧<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>刻在墙体中<span><span>？</span></span>那石门后面究竟是什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>莫家墓陵<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫连风一字一字说罢<span><span>，</span></span>沉沉叹了口气<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>原是莫家的墓…<span><span>」</span></span> 我兀自念叨着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>忽然<span><span>，</span></span>莫连风一个抬眼<span><span>，</span></span>眼神中古怪的锋芒让我莫名怔了一下<span><span>。</span></span>下一秒<span><span>，</span></span>他冷幽幽问道<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>石门后面<span><span>，</span></span>那主墓的墙壁上挂着一幅人像<span><span>。</span></span>林大人想看看么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我淡淡回道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不想<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风一顿<span><span>，</span></span>似是没想到我会如此没有好奇心<span><span>。</span></span>片刻<span><span>，</span></span>他轻轻笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那我换个问题<span><span>，</span></span>三千年前<span><span>，</span></span>林大人身在何处<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>地府<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我冷冷道<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>是么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 莫连风紧紧盯着我的眼睛<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不是在人间么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>胡言乱语<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我冷眼看着莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>毫不客气<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风古怪得笑了一下<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是不是胡言乱语<span><span>，</span></span>只有林大人心中才有答案<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>他的这句话<span><span>，</span></span>我听得不清不楚<span><span>，</span></span>直到我随他进入石门<span><span>，</span></span>在那主墓的墙壁上见到那幅人像<span><span>，</span></span>才逐渐有了清晰的轮廓<span><span>。</span></span>明白了他为何最初见我便眼神怨怼<span><span>，</span></span>为何言语之中透着强烈的<span><span>、</span></span>难以掩饰的埋怨<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>幽暗阴冷的墓室中<span><span>，</span></span>橘色的烛火轻轻跳跃<span><span>，</span></span>画像前燃着的香火烧得正旺<span><span>，</span></span>徐徐冒出淡淡烟雾<span><span>。</span></span>透过层层交织的烟气与光圈<span><span>，</span></span>我终于看清了那挂在墙壁上的人像<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那怀抱琵琶<span><span>，</span></span>安静端坐<span><span>，</span></span>嘴角带着笑意<span><span>，</span></span>眼神却无比冷淡的女子<span><span>，</span></span>竟是我自己<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <h2><span><span>【</span></span>21<span><span>】</span></span></h2>
 <p>盯着那画像<span><span>，</span></span>我许久没有说话<span><span>。</span></span>我在回忆着过去几千年漫长的时光中<span><span>，</span></span>究竟是否有这样的一瞬<span><span>，</span></span>我怀抱琵琶<span><span>，</span></span>静静端坐<span><span>，</span></span>望着那正画着我的某个人<span><span>，</span></span>强装着笑意<span><span>，</span></span>眼中却暗暗压抑着刺骨的冰寒<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>其实我想到了一个人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可是莫连风忽然开口<span><span>，</span></span>声音幽幽<span><span>，</span></span>打断了我的思绪<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>吾莫家先祖<span><span>，</span></span>莫镜云<span><span>，</span></span>林大人可认得<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>谁<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span> 我忽然看向莫连风<span><span>，</span></span>心中一震<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>莫连风重复道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>三千年前楚国的虎林军统领<span><span>，</span></span>雪桑谷第一任谷主<span><span>，</span></span>莫镜云<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我盯着莫连风<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>莫镜云是你家祖上<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我心中一沉<span><span>。</span></span>莫镜云…惜娘…殷如惜…原来是她<span><span>，</span></span>是他们…</p>
 <p>莫连风眼角一颤<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>看来林大人还记得<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我没有回答<span><span>，</span></span>只是冷淡得说了三个字<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怪不得<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
</body>
